gita_verse:6.9	<center><big>सुहृन्मित्रार्युदासीनमध्यस्थद्वेष्यबन्धुषु।<br><br>साधुष्वपि च पापेषु समबुद्धिर्विशिष्यते।।6.9।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>suhṛin-mitrāryudāsīna-madhyastha-dveṣhya-bandhuṣhu<br>sādhuṣhvapi cha pāpeṣhu sama-buddhir viśhiṣhyate<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>He excels who has sameness of view with regard to a benefactor, a friend, an enemy, a neutral, an arbiter, the hateful, a relative, good people, and even sinners.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>He who is of the same mind towards the good-hearted, friends, enemies, the indifferent, the neutral, the hateful, the relatives, the righteous, and the unrighteous, excels.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_9.mp3]
gita_verse:6.10	<center><big>योगी युञ्जीत सततमात्मानं रहसि स्थितः।<br><br>एकाकी यतचित्तात्मा निराशीरपरिग्रहः।।6.10।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>yogī yuñjīta satatam ātmānaṁ rahasi sthitaḥ<br>ekākī yata-chittātmā nirāśhīr aparigrahaḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>A yogi should constantly concentrate his mind by staying in a solitary place, alone, with mind and body controlled, free from expectations, and free from acquisition.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Let the yogi constantly strive to keep the mind steady, remaining in solitude, alone, with the body and mind controlled, and free from hope and greed.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_10.mp3]
gita_verse:6.11	<center><big>शुचौ देशे प्रतिष्ठाप्य स्थिरमासनमात्मनः।<br><br>नात्युच्छ्रितं नातिनीचं चैलाजिनकुशोत्तरम्।।6.11।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>śhuchau deśhe pratiṣhṭhāpya sthiram āsanam ātmanaḥ<br>nātyuchchhritaṁ nāti-nīchaṁ chailājina-kuśhottaram<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Having firmly established in a clean place his seat, neither too high nor too low, composed of cloth, skin, and kusa-grass placed successively one below the other;<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>In a clean spot, having established a firm seat of his own, neither too high nor too low, made of cloth, skin, and kusha grass layered one over the other.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_11.mp3]
gita_verse:6.12-13	<center><big>तत्रैकाग्रं मनः कृत्वा यतचित्तेन्द्रियक्रियः।<br><br>उपविश्यासने युञ्ज्याद्योगमात्मविशुद्धये।।6.12।।<br> <br><br>समं कायशिरोग्रीवं धारयन्नचलं स्थिरः।<br><br>संप्रेक्ष्य नासिकाग्रं स्वं दिशश्चानवलोकयन्।।6.13।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>tatraikāgraṁ manaḥ kṛitvā yata-chittendriya-kriyaḥ<br>upaviśhyāsane yuñjyād yogam ātma-viśhuddhaye<br><br>samaṁ kāya-śhiro-grīvaṁ dhārayann achalaṁ sthiraḥ<br>samprekṣhya nāsikāgraṁ svaṁ diśhaśh chānavalokayan<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Sitting on that seat, he should concentrate his mind for the purification of the internal organ, making the mind one-pointed and keeping the actions of the mind and senses under control. Holding the body, head, and neck erect and still, being steady, looking at the tip of his own nose and not looking around.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>There, having made the mind one-pointed, with the actions of the mind and senses controlled, let him, seated on the seat, practice Yoga for the purification of the self. Let him firmly hold his body, head, and neck erect and still, gazing at the tip of his nose without looking around.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_12-13.mp3]
gita_verse:6.14	<center><big>प्रशान्तात्मा विगतभीर्ब्रह्मचारिव्रते स्थितः।<br><br>मनः संयम्य मच्चित्तो युक्त आसीत मत्परः।।6.14।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>praśhāntātmā vigata-bhīr brahmachāri-vrate sthitaḥ<br>manaḥ sanyamya mach-chitto yukta āsīta mat-paraḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>He should remain seated with a placid mind, free from fear, firm in the vow of celibacy, and with the mind fixed on Me by controlling it through concentration, having Me as the supreme goal.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Serene-minded, fearless, firm in the vow of a Brahmachari, having controlled their mind, thinking of Me and balanced in mind, let them sit, having Me as their supreme goal.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_14.mp3]
gita_verse:6.15	<center><big>युञ्जन्नेवं सदाऽऽत्मानं योगी नियतमानसः।<br><br>शान्तिं निर्वाणपरमां मत्संस्थामधिगच्छति।।6.15।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>yuñjann evaṁ sadātmānaṁ yogī niyata-mānasaḥ<br>śhantiṁ nirvāṇa-paramāṁ mat-sansthām adhigachchhati<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Concentrating the mind thus, forever, the yogi of a controlled mind achieves the peace that culminates in liberation and abides in Me.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Thus, always keeping the mind balanced, the yogi, with the mind controlled, attains the peace abiding in Me, culminating in liberation.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_15.mp3]
gita_verse:6.16	<center><big>नात्यश्नतस्तु योगोऽस्ति न चैकान्तमनश्नतः।<br><br>न चातिस्वप्नशीलस्य जाग्रतो नैव चार्जुन।।6.16।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>nātyaśhnatastu yogo ’sti na chaikāntam anaśhnataḥ<br>na chāti-svapna-śhīlasya jāgrato naiva chārjuna<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>But, O Arjuna, Yoga is not for one who eats excessively, nor for one who does not eat at all; neither for one who habitually sleeps too long, nor for one who stays awake.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Verily, Yoga is not possible for him who eats too much, nor for him who does not eat at all, nor for him who sleeps too much, nor for him who is always awake, O Arjuna.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_16.mp3]
gita_verse:6.17	<center><big>युक्ताहारविहारस्य युक्तचेष्टस्य कर्मसु।<br><br>युक्तस्वप्नावबोधस्य योगो भवति दुःखहा।।6.17।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>yuktāhāra-vihārasya yukta-cheṣhṭasya karmasu<br>yukta-svapnāvabodhasya yogo bhavati duḥkha-hā<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Yoga becomes a destroyer of sorrow for one whose eating and movements are regulated, whose effort in works is moderate, and whose sleep and wakefulness are temperate.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Yoga becomes the destroyer of pain for him who is moderate in eating and recreation (such as walking, etc.), who exercises moderation in action, and who is moderate in sleep and wakefulness.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_17.mp3]
gita_verse:6.18	<center><big>यदा विनियतं चित्तमात्मन्येवावतिष्ठते।<br><br>निःस्पृहः सर्वकामेभ्यो युक्त इत्युच्यते तदा।।6.18।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>yadā viniyataṁ chittam ātmanyevāvatiṣhṭhate<br>niḥspṛihaḥ sarva-kāmebhyo yukta ityuchyate tadā<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>A person who has become free from hankering for all desirable objects is said to be Self-absorbed when the controlled mind rests solely in the Self.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>When the perfectly controlled mind rests in the Self alone, free from longing for any of the objects of desire, then it is said, 'He is united'.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_18.mp3]
gita_verse:6.19	<center><big>यथा दीपो निवातस्थो नेङ्गते सोपमा स्मृता।<br><br>योगिनो यतचित्तस्य युञ्जतो योगमात्मनः।।6.19।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>yathā dīpo nivāta-stho neṅgate sopamā smṛitā<br>yogino yata-chittasya yuñjato yogam ātmanaḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>As a lamp kept in a windless place does not flicker, so is the simile for the yogi whose mind is under control and who is engaged in concentration on the Self.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>As a lamp placed in a windless spot does not flicker, so is the Yogi of a controlled mind, who practices Yoga in the Self, compared.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_19.mp3]
gita_verse:6.20	<center><big>यत्रोपरमते चित्तं निरुद्धं योगसेवया।<br><br>यत्र चैवात्मनाऽऽत्मानं पश्यन्नात्मनि तुष्यति।।6.20।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>yatroparamate chittaṁ niruddhaṁ yoga-sevayā<br>yatra chaivātmanātmānaṁ paśhyann ātmani tuṣhyati<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>At the time when the mind, restrained through the practice of Yoga, is withdrawn, and just when one sees the Self by the self and remains contented in the Self alone;<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>When the mind, restrained by the practice of yoga, attains quietude, and when one sees the Self by the Self, they are satisfied in their own Self.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_20.mp3]
gita_verse:6.21	<center><big>सुखमात्यन्तिकं यत्तद्बुद्धिग्राह्यमतीन्द्रियम्।<br><br>वेत्ति यत्र न चैवायं स्थितश्चलति तत्त्वतः।।6.21।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>sukham ātyantikaṁ yat tad buddhi-grāhyam atīndriyam<br>vetti yatra na chaivāyaṁ sthitaśh chalati tattvataḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>When one experiences that absolute Bliss, which can be intuited by the intellect and which is beyond the senses, and being thus established, this person surely does not swerve from Reality.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>When he (the Yogi) feels that infinite bliss which can be grasped by the pure intellect and which transcends the senses, and is established therein, never moving away from the reality.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_21.mp3]
gita_verse:6.22	<center><big>यं लब्ध्वा चापरं लाभं मन्यते नाधिकं ततः।<br><br>यस्मिन्स्थितो न दुःखेन गुरुणापि विचाल्यते।।6.22।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>yaṁ labdhvā chāparaṁ lābhaṁ manyate nādhikaṁ tataḥ<br>yasmin sthito na duḥkhena guruṇāpi vichālyate<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Obtaining which one does not consider any other acquisition to be superior, and being established in which one is not perturbed even by great sorrow;<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Having obtained it, he thinks there is no other gain superior to it; established in it, he is not moved even by heavy sorrow.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_22.mp3]
gita_verse:6.23	<center><big>तं विद्याद् दुःखसंयोगवियोगं योगसंज्ञितम्।<br><br>स निश्चयेन योक्तव्यो योगोऽनिर्विण्णचेतसा।।6.23।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>taṁ vidyād duḥkha-sanyoga-viyogaṁ yogasaṅjñitam<br>sa niśhchayena yoktavyo yogo ’nirviṇṇa-chetasā<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>One should know that severance of contact with sorrow to be what is called Yoga. That Yoga should be practiced with perseverance and with an undepressed heart.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Let this be known by the name of Yoga, the severance from union with pain. This Yoga should be practiced with determination and with an undespairing mind.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_23.mp3]
gita_verse:6.24-25	<center><big>सङ्कल्पप्रभवान्कामांस्त्यक्त्वा सर्वानशेषतः।<br><br>मनसैवेन्द्रियग्रामं विनियम्य समन्ततः।।6.24।।<br> <br><br>शनैः शनैरुपरमेद् बुद्ध्या धृतिगृहीतया।<br><br>आत्मसंस्थं मनः कृत्वा न किञ्चिदपि चिन्तयेत्।।6.25।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>saṅkalpa-prabhavān kāmāns tyaktvā sarvān aśheṣhataḥ<br>manasaivendriya-grāmaṁ viniyamya samantataḥ<br><br>śhanaiḥ śhanair uparamed buddhyā dhṛiti-gṛihītayā<br>ātma-sansthaṁ manaḥ kṛitvā na kiñchid api chintayet<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>By totally eschewing all desires that arise from thoughts and restraining all the organs with the mind from every side; One should gradually withdraw with the intellect, endowed with steadiness. Making the mind fixed in the Self, one should not think of anything at all.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Abandoning unreservedly all desires born of Sankalpa (thought and imagination) and completely restraining the whole group of senses by the mind from all sides. Little by little, let him attain steadiness of the intellect by holding it firmly; having made the mind establish itself in the Self, let him not think of anything else.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_24-25.mp3]
gita_verse:6.26	<center><big>यतो यतो निश्चरति मनश्चञ्चलमस्थिरम्।<br><br>ततस्ततो नियम्यैतदात्मन्येव वशं नयेत्।।6.26।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>yato yato niśhcharati manaśh chañchalam asthiram<br>tatas tato niyamyaitad ātmanyeva vaśhaṁ nayet<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>The yogi should bring this mind under the subjugation of the Self itself, restraining it from all those causes that cause the restless, unsteady mind to wander away.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>From whatever cause the restless and unsteady mind wanders away, let him restrain it from that and bring it under the control of the Self alone.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_26.mp3]
gita_verse:6.27	<center><big>प्रशान्तमनसं ह्येनं योगिनं सुखमुत्तमम्।<br><br>उपैति शान्तरजसं ब्रह्मभूतमकल्मषम्।।6.27।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>praśhānta-manasaṁ hyenaṁ yoginaṁ sukham uttamam<br>upaiti śhānta-rajasaṁ brahma-bhūtam akalmaṣham<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Supreme Bliss comes to this yogi alone whose mind has become perfectly tranquil, whose quality of rajas has been eliminated, who has become identified with Brahman, and is untainted.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Supreme Bliss indeed comes to this Yogi whose mind is made peaceful, whose passion is quelled, who has become Brahman, and who is free from sin.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_27.mp3]
gita_verse:6.28	<center><big>युञ्जन्नेवं सदाऽऽत्मानं योगी विगतकल्मषः।<br><br>सुखेन ब्रह्मसंस्पर्शमत्यन्तं सुखमश्नुते।।6.28।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>yuñjann evaṁ sadātmānaṁ yogī vigata-kalmaṣhaḥ<br>sukhena brahma-sansparśham atyantaṁ sukham aśhnute<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>By constantly concentrating his mind in this way, the taintless yogi easily attains the absolute bliss of contact with Brahman.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>The yogi, always engaging the mind thus (in the practice of yoga), is freed from sins and easily enjoys the infinite bliss of contact with Brahman (the Eternal).<br><br>[sound:gita_6_28.mp3]
gita_verse:6.29	<center><big>सर्वभूतस्थमात्मानं सर्वभूतानि चात्मनि।<br><br>ईक्षते योगयुक्तात्मा सर्वत्र समदर्शनः।।6.29।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>sarva-bhūta-stham ātmānaṁ sarva-bhūtāni chātmani<br>īkṣhate yoga-yuktātmā sarvatra sama-darśhanaḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>One who has their mind Self-absorbed through Yoga, and who has the vision of sameness everywhere, sees this Self existing in everything, and everything in their Self.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>With the mind harmonized by Yoga, he sees the Self abiding in all beings and all beings in the Self; he sees the same everywhere.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_29.mp3]
gita_verse:6.30	<center><big>यो मां पश्यति सर्वत्र सर्वं च मयि पश्यति।<br><br>तस्याहं न प्रणश्यामि स च मे न प्रणश्यति।।6.30।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>yo māṁ paśhyati sarvatra sarvaṁ cha mayi paśhyati<br>tasyāhaṁ na praṇaśhyāmi sa cha me na praṇaśhyati<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>One who sees Me in everything and sees all things in Me—I do not lose sight of him, and he also is not lost to My vision.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>He who sees Me everywhere and sees everything in Me, never becomes separated from Me, nor do I from him.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_30.mp3]
gita_verse:6.31	<center><big>सर्वभूतस्थितं यो मां भजत्येकत्वमास्थितः।<br><br>सर्वथा वर्तमानोऽपि स योगी मयि वर्तते।।6.31।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>sarva-bhūta-sthitaṁ yo māṁ bhajatyekatvam āsthitaḥ<br>sarvathā vartamāno ’pi sa yogī mayi vartate<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>That yogi, who, being established in unity, adores Me as existing in all things, exists in Me—in whatever condition he may be.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>He who, being established in unity, worships Me, who dwells in all beings, that yogi abides in Me, whatever their mode of living may be.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_31.mp3]
gita_verse:6.32	<center><big>आत्मौपम्येन सर्वत्र समं पश्यति योऽर्जुन।<br><br>सुखं वा यदि वा दुःखं सः योगी परमो मतः।।6.32।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>ātmaupamyena sarvatra samaṁ paśhyati yo ’rjuna<br>sukhaṁ vā yadi vā duḥkhaṁ sa yogī paramo mataḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O Arjuna, that yogi is considered the best who judges what is happiness and sorrow in all beings by the same standard as they would apply to themselves.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>He who, through the likeness of the Self, O Arjuna, sees reality everywhere, be it pleasure or pain, is regarded as the highest Yogi.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_32.mp3]
gita_verse:6.33	<center><big>अर्जुन उवाच<br><br>योऽयं योगस्त्वया प्रोक्तः साम्येन मधुसूदन।<br><br>एतस्याहं न पश्यामि चञ्चलत्वात् स्थितिं स्थिराम्।।6.33।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>arjuna uvācha<br>yo ’yaṁ yogas tvayā proktaḥ sāmyena madhusūdana<br>etasyāhaṁ na paśhyāmi chañchalatvāt sthitiṁ sthirām<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Arjuna said, "O Madhusudana (Krsna), this Yoga that You have spoken of as sameness, I do not see its steady continuance due to the restlessness of the mind."<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Arjuna said, "O Krishna, I do not see how this Yoga of equanimity, which you have taught me, can be maintained steadily, due to the restlessness of the mind."<br><br>[sound:gita_6_33.mp3]
gita_verse:6.34	<center><big>चञ्चलं हि मनः कृष्ण प्रमाथि बलवद्दृढम्।<br><br>तस्याहं निग्रहं मन्ये वायोरिव सुदुष्करम्।।6.34।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>chañchalaṁ hi manaḥ kṛiṣhṇa pramāthi balavad dṛiḍham<br>tasyāhaṁ nigrahaṁ manye vāyor iva su-duṣhkaram<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>For, O Kṛṣṇa, the mind is unsteady, turbulent, strong, and obstinate; I consider its control to be as difficult as that of the wind.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>The mind is indeed restless, turbulent, strong, and unyielding, O Krishna; I consider it as difficult to control as controlling the wind.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_34.mp3]
gita_verse:6.35	<center><big>श्री भगवानुवाच<br><br>असंशयं महाबाहो मनो दुर्निग्रहं चलं।<br><br>अभ्यासेन तु कौन्तेय वैराग्येण च गृह्यते।।6.35।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>śhrī bhagavān uvācha<br>asanśhayaṁ mahā-bāho mano durnigrahaṁ chalam<br>abhyāsena tu kaunteya vairāgyeṇa cha gṛihyate<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>The Blessed Lord said, O mighty-armed one, undoubtedly the mind is untamable and restless. But, O son of Kunti, it can be brought under control through practice and detachment.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>The Blessed Lord said, "Undoubtedly, O mighty-armed Arjuna, the mind is difficult to control and restless; but with practice and dispassion, it can be restrained."<br><br>[sound:gita_6_35.mp3]
gita_verse:6.36	<center><big>असंयतात्मना योगो दुष्प्राप इति मे मतिः।<br><br>वश्यात्मना तु यतता शक्योऽवाप्तुमुपायतः।।6.36।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>asaṅyatātmanā yogo duṣhprāpa iti me matiḥ<br>vaśhyātmanā tu yatatā śhakyo ’vāptum upāyataḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>My conviction is that Yoga is difficult to attain for one with an uncontrolled mind. But it is possible to attain through the aforementioned means for one who strives and has a controlled mind.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>I think Yoga is hard to be attained by one with an uncontrolled self, but the self-controlled and striving one can attain it by the appropriate means.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_36.mp3]
gita_verse:6.37	<center><big>अर्जुन उवाच<br><br>अयतिः श्रद्धयोपेतो योगाच्चलितमानसः।<br><br>अप्राप्य योगसंसिद्धिं कां गतिं कृष्ण गच्छति।।6.37।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>arjuna uvācha<br>ayatiḥ śhraddhayopeto yogāch chalita-mānasaḥ<br>aprāpya yoga-sansiddhiṁ kāṅ gatiṁ kṛiṣhṇa gachchhati<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Arjuna said, "O Krsna, what goal does one attain who, despite having faith, fails to achieve perfection in Yoga due to lack of diligence, and whose mind becomes deflected from Yoga?"<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Arjuna said, "He who is unable to control himself, even though he has faith, and whose mind wanders away from Yoga, what end does he meet, having failed to attain perfection in Yoga, O Krishna?"<br><br>[sound:gita_6_37.mp3]
gita_verse:6.38	<center><big>कच्चिन्नोभयविभ्रष्टश्छिन्नाभ्रमिव नश्यति।<br><br>अप्रतिष्ठो महाबाहो विमूढो ब्रह्मणः पथि।।6.38।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>kachchin nobhaya-vibhraṣhṭaśh chhinnābhram iva naśhyati<br>apratiṣhṭho mahā-bāho vimūḍho brahmaṇaḥ pathi<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O Mighty-armed one, having fallen from both [paths], without support, deluded on the path to Brahman, does he not get ruined like a scattered cloud?<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Fallen from both, does he not perish like a rent cloud, supportless, O mighty-armed one, deluded on the path of Brahman?<br><br>[sound:gita_6_38.mp3]
gita_verse:6.39	<center><big>एतन्मे संशयं कृष्ण छेत्तुमर्हस्यशेषतः।<br><br>त्वदन्यः संशयस्यास्य छेत्ता न ह्युपपद्यते।।6.39।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>etan me sanśhayaṁ kṛiṣhṇa chhettum arhasyaśheṣhataḥ<br>tvad-anyaḥ sanśhayasyāsya chhettā na hyupapadyate<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O Krsna, you should totally eradicate this doubt of mine, for none other than yourself can be the dispeller of this doubt!<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>O Krishna, please completely dispel this doubt of mine, for it is not possible for anyone but You to do so.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_39.mp3]
gita_verse:6.40	<center><big>श्री भगवानुवाच<br><br>पार्थ नैवेह नामुत्र विनाशस्तस्य विद्यते।<br><br>नहि कल्याणकृत्कश्िचद्दुर्गतिं तात गच्छति।।6.40।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>śhrī bhagavān uvācha<br>pārtha naiveha nāmutra vināśhas tasya vidyate<br>na hi kalyāṇa-kṛit kaśhchid durgatiṁ tāta gachchhati<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>The Blessed Lord said, "O Partha, there is certainly no ruin for him here or hereafter, for no one engaged in good meets with a deplorable end, my son!"<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>The Blessed Lord said, "O Arjuna, neither in this world nor in the next will there be destruction for him; none, indeed, who does good, O my son, ever comes to grief."<br><br>[sound:gita_6_40.mp3]
gita_verse:6.41-42	<center><big>प्राप्य पुण्यकृतां लोकानुषित्वा शाश्वतीः समाः।<br><br>शुचीनां श्रीमतां गेहे योगभ्रष्टोऽभिजायते।।6.41।।<br> <br><br>अथवा योगिनामेव कुले भवति धीमताम्।<br><br>एतद्धि दुर्लभतरं लोके जन्म यदीदृशम्।।6.42।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>prāpya puṇya-kṛitāṁ lokān uṣhitvā śhāśhvatīḥ samāḥ<br>śhuchīnāṁ śhrīmatāṁ gehe yoga-bhraṣhṭo’bhijāyate<br><br>atha vā yoginām eva kule bhavati dhīmatām<br>etad dhi durlabhataraṁ loke janma yad īdṛiśham<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Attaining the worlds of the righteous and residing there for eternal years, the man who has fallen from Yoga is born in the house of the pious and prosperous. Or, he is born in the family of wise yogis. Such a birth is indeed more difficult to come by in the world.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Having attained to the worlds of the righteous and having dwelt there for everlasting years, he who fell from Yoga is born in a house of the pure and wealthy. Or he is born in a family of even the wisest of yogis; verily, such a birth is very difficult to obtain in this world.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_41-42.mp3]
gita_verse:6.43	<center><big>तत्र तं बुद्धिसंयोगं लभते पौर्वदेहिकम्।<br><br>यतते च ततो भूयः संसिद्धौ कुरुनन्दन।।6.43।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>tatra taṁ buddhi-sanyogaṁ labhate paurva-dehikam<br>yatate cha tato bhūyaḥ sansiddhau kuru-nandana<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>There he becomes endowed with the wisdom acquired in the previous body, and he strives even more than before for perfection, O scion of the Kuru dynasty.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Then he comes into contact with the knowledge acquired in his former body and strives even more for perfection, O Arjuna.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_43.mp3]
gita_verse:6.44	<center><big>पूर्वाभ्यासेन तेनैव ह्रियते ह्यवशोऽपि सः।<br><br>जिज्ञासुरपि योगस्य शब्दब्रह्मातिवर्तते।।6.44।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>pūrvābhyāsena tenaiva hriyate hyavaśho ’pi saḥ<br>jijñāsur api yogasya śhabda-brahmātivartate<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>For, by that very past practice, he is carried forward even in spite of himself! Even a seeker of Yoga transcends the results of the performance of Vedic rituals!<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>By that same former practice, he is borne on in spite of himself. Even he who merely wishes to know Yoga goes beyond the Brahmanic word.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_44.mp3]
gita_verse:6.45	<center><big>प्रयत्नाद्यतमानस्तु योगी संशुद्धकिल्बिषः।<br><br>अनेकजन्मसंसिद्धस्ततो याति परां गतिम्।।6.45।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>prayatnād yatamānas tu yogī sanśhuddha-kilbiṣhaḥ<br>aneka-janma-sansiddhas tato yāti parāṁ gatim<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>However, the yogi, applying himself assiduously, becoming purified from sin and attaining perfection through many births, they achieve the highest Goal.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>But the Yogi who strives assiduously, purified of sins and perfected gradually over many births, reaches the highest goal.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_45.mp3]
gita_verse:6.46	<center><big>तपस्विभ्योऽधिको योगी ज्ञानिभ्योऽपि मतोऽधिकः।<br><br>कर्मिभ्यश्चाधिको योगी तस्माद्योगी भवार्जुन।।6.46।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>tapasvibhyo ’dhiko yogī<br>jñānibhyo ’pi mato ’dhikaḥ<br>karmibhyaśh chādhiko yogī<br>tasmād yogī bhavārjuna<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>A yogi is higher than those of austerity; they are considered higher even than those of knowledge. The yogi is also higher than those of action. Therefore, O Arjuna, become a yogi.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>The yogi is thought to be superior to the ascetics, even superior to those who have knowledge obtained through the study of scriptures; he is also superior to men of action; therefore, be thou a yogi, O Arjuna.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_46.mp3]
gita_verse:6.47	<center><big>योगिनामपि सर्वेषां मद्गतेनान्तरात्मना।<br><br>श्रद्धावान्भजते यो मां स मे युक्ततमो मतः।।6.47।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>yoginām api sarveṣhāṁ mad-gatenāntar-ātmanā<br>śhraddhāvān bhajate yo māṁ sa me yuktatamo mataḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Even among all the yogis, he who adores Me with his mind fixed on Me and with faith is considered by Me to be the best of the yogis.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>And among all the Yogis, he who, full of faith and with his inner self merged in Me, worships Me is deemed by Me to be the most devoted.<br><br>[sound:gita_6_47.mp3]
gita_verse:7.1	<center><big>श्री भगवानुवाच<br><br>मय्यासक्तमनाः पार्थ योगं युञ्जन्मदाश्रयः।<br><br>असंशयं समग्रं मां यथा ज्ञास्यसि तच्छृणु।।7.1।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>śhrī bhagavān uvācha<br>mayyāsakta-manāḥ pārtha yogaṁ yuñjan mad-āśhrayaḥ<br>asanśhayaṁ samagraṁ māṁ yathā jñāsyasi tach chhṛiṇu<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>The Blessed Lord said, "O Partha, hear how, with your mind fixed on Me, practicing the Yoga of Meditation and taking refuge in Me, you will certainly and fully know Me.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>The Blessed Lord said, "O Arjuna, hear how you shall, without doubt, know Me fully, with your mind intent on Me, practicing Yoga and taking refuge in Me."<br><br>[sound:gita_7_1.mp3]
gita_verse:7.2	<center><big>ज्ञानं तेऽहं सविज्ञानमिदं वक्ष्याम्यशेषतः।<br><br>यज्ज्ञात्वा नेह भूयोऽन्यज्ज्ञातव्यमवशिष्यते।।7.2।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>jñānaṁ te ’haṁ sa-vijñānam idaṁ vakṣhyāmyaśheṣhataḥ<br>yaj jñātvā neha bhūyo ’nyaj jñātavyam-avaśhiṣhyate<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>I shall tell you in detail of this Knowledge, which is combined with realization, after experiencing which there remains nothing else here to be known.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>I will declare to you in full this knowledge combined with realization, after knowing which nothing else remains to be known here.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_2.mp3]
gita_verse:7.3	<center><big>मनुष्याणां सहस्रेषु कश्िचद्यतति सिद्धये।<br><br>यततामपि सिद्धानां कश्िचन्मां वेत्ति तत्त्वतः।।7.3।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>manuṣhyāṇāṁ sahasreṣhu kaśhchid yatati siddhaye<br>yatatām api siddhānāṁ kaśhchin māṁ vetti tattvataḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Among thousands of men, a rare one endeavors for perfection. gita_verse:7.4	<center><big>भूमिरापोऽनलो वायुः खं मनो बुद्धिरेव च।<br><br>अहङ्कार इतीयं मे भिन्ना प्रकृतिरष्टधा।।7.4।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>bhūmir-āpo ’nalo vāyuḥ khaṁ mano buddhir eva cha<br>ahankāra itīyaṁ me bhinnā prakṛitir aṣhṭadhā<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>This Prakrti of Mine is divided eightfold thus: earth, water, fire, air, space, mind, intellect, and egoism.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Earth, water, fire, air, ether, mind, intellect, and egoism—thus is My Nature divided eightfold.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_4.mp3]
gita_verse:7.5	<center><big>अपरेयमितस्त्वन्यां प्रकृतिं विद्धि मे पराम्।<br><br>जीवभूतां महाबाहो ययेदं धार्यते जगत्।।7.5।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>apareyam itas tvanyāṁ prakṛitiṁ viddhi me parām<br>jīva-bhūtāṁ mahā-bāho yayedaṁ dhāryate jagat<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O mighty-armed one, this is the inferior Prakrti. Know the other Prakrti of Mine, which is however higher than this, which has taken the form of individual souls, and by which this world is upheld.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>O mighty-armed Arjuna, this is the inferior Prakriti; know it as distinct from My higher Prakriti, the very life-element, by which this world is upheld.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_5.mp3]
gita_verse:7.6	<center><big>एतद्योनीनि भूतानि सर्वाणीत्युपधारय।<br><br>अहं कृत्स्नस्य जगतः प्रभवः प्रलयस्तथा।।7.6।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>etad-yonīni bhūtāni sarvāṇītyupadhāraya<br>ahaṁ kṛitsnasya jagataḥ prabhavaḥ pralayas tathā<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Understand thus that all things—sentient and insentient—have these as their source. I am the origin as well as the end of the entire universe.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Know that these two are the womb of all beings; thus, I am the source and dissolution of the whole universe.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_6.mp3]
gita_verse:7.7	<center><big>मत्तः परतरं नान्यत्किञ्चिदस्ति धनञ्जय।<br><br>मयि सर्वमिदं प्रोतं सूत्रे मणिगणा इव।।7.7।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>mattaḥ parataraṁ nānyat kiñchid asti dhanañjaya<br>mayi sarvam idaṁ protaṁ sūtre maṇi-gaṇā iva<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O Dhananjaya, there is nothing else higher than Myself. All this is strung on Me, like clusters of gems on a string.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_7.mp3]
gita_verse:7.8	<center><big>रसोऽहमप्सु कौन्तेय प्रभास्मि शशिसूर्ययोः।<br><br>प्रणवः सर्ववेदेषु शब्दः खे पौरुषं नृषु।।7.8।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>raso ’ham apsu kaunteya prabhāsmi śhaśhi-sūryayoḥ<br>praṇavaḥ sarva-vedeṣhu śhabdaḥ khe pauruṣhaṁ nṛiṣhu<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O son of Kunti, I am the taste of water, I am the effulgence of the moon and the sun; the letter 'Om' in all the Vedas, the sound in space, and manhood in men.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>I am the flavor in water, O Arjuna; I am the light in the moon and the sun; I am the syllable Om in all the Vedas, sound in the ether and virility in men.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_8.mp3]
gita_verse:7.9	<center><big>पुण्यो गन्धः पृथिव्यां च तेजश्चास्मि विभावसौ।<br><br>जीवनं सर्वभूतेषु तपश्चास्मि तपस्विषु।।7.9।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>puṇyo gandhaḥ pṛithivyāṁ cha tejaśh chāsmi vibhāvasau<br>jīvanaṁ sarva-bhūteṣhu tapaśh chāsmi tapasviṣhu<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>I am also the sweet fragrance in the earth; I am the brilliance in the fire, and the life in all beings; and I am the austerity of the ascetics.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>I am the sweet fragrance in the earth and the brilliance in the fire, the life in all beings, and I am the austerity of ascetics.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_9.mp3]
gita_verse:7.10	<center><big>बीजं मां सर्वभूतानां विद्धि पार्थ सनातनम्।<br><br>बुद्धिर्बुद्धिमतामस्मि तेजस्तेजस्विनामहम्।।7.10।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>bījaṁ māṁ sarva-bhūtānāṁ viddhi pārtha sanātanam<br>buddhir buddhimatām asmi tejas tejasvinām aham<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O Partha, know Me to be the eternal seed of all beings. gita_verse:7.11	<center><big>बलं बलवतां चाहं कामरागविवर्जितम्।<br><br>धर्माविरुद्धो भूतेषु कामोऽस्मि भरतर्षभ।।7.11।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>balaṁ balavatāṁ chāhaṁ kāma-rāga-vivarjitam<br>dharmāviruddho bhūteṣhu kāmo ’smi bharatarṣhabha<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>And of the strong, I am the strength that is devoid of passion and attachment. gita_verse:7.12	<center><big>ये चैव सात्त्विका भावा राजसास्तामसाश्च ये।<br><br>मत्त एवेति तान्विद्धि नत्वहं तेषु ते मयि।।7.12।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>ye chaiva sāttvikā bhāvā rājasās tāmasāśh cha ye<br>matta eveti tān viddhi na tvahaṁ teṣhu te mayi<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Those things that are made of the quality of sattva, and those things that are made of the quality of rajas and tamas, know them to have sprung from Me alone. They are in Me, yet I am not in them.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_12.mp3]
gita_verse:7.13	<center><big>त्रिभिर्गुणमयैर्भावैरेभिः सर्वमिदं जगत्।<br><br>मोहितं नाभिजानाति मामेभ्यः परमव्ययम्।।7.13।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>tribhir guṇa-mayair bhāvair ebhiḥ sarvam idaṁ jagat<br>mohitaṁ nābhijānāti māmebhyaḥ param avyayam<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>All this world, deluded as it is by these three qualities made of the gunas, does not know Me, who am transcendental to these and undecaying.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Deluded by these Natures, composed of the three qualities of Nature, all this world does not know Me as distinct from them and immutable.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_13.mp3]
gita_verse:7.14	<center><big>दैवी ह्येषा गुणमयी मम माया दुरत्यया।<br><br>मामेव ये प्रपद्यन्ते मायामेतां तरन्ति ते।।7.14।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>daivī hyeṣhā guṇa-mayī mama māyā duratyayā<br>mām eva ye prapadyante māyām etāṁ taranti te<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Since this divine Maya of Mine, which is constituted by the gunas, is difficult to cross over, those who take refuge in Me alone can transcend this Maya.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Verily, this divine illusion of Mine, composed of the three qualities, is difficult to cross over; those who take refuge in Me alone, can cross over this illusion.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_14.mp3]
gita_verse:7.15	<center><big>न मां दुष्कृतिनो मूढाः प्रपद्यन्ते नराधमाः।<br><br>माययापहृतज्ञाना आसुरं भावमाश्रिताः।।7.15।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>na māṁ duṣhkṛitino mūḍhāḥ prapadyante narādhamāḥ<br>māyayāpahṛita-jñānā āsuraṁ bhāvam āśhritāḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>The foolish evildoers, who are the most depraved among men, who are deprived of their wisdom by Maya, and who resort to demonic ways, do not take refuge in Me.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>The evil-doers and the deluded, who are the lowest of men, do not seek Me; those whose knowledge is destroyed by illusion follow the ways of demons.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_15.mp3]
gita_verse:7.16	<center><big>चतुर्विधा भजन्ते मां जनाः सुकृतिनोऽर्जुन।<br><br>आर्तो जिज्ञासुरर्थार्थी ज्ञानी च भरतर्षभ।।7.16।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>chatur-vidhā bhajante māṁ janāḥ sukṛitino ’rjuna<br>ārto jijñāsur arthārthī jñānī cha bharatarṣhabha<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O Arjuna, foremost of the Bharata dynasty, four classes of people of virtuous deeds adore Me: the afflicted, the seekers of Knowledge, the seekers of wealth, and the man of Knowledge.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Four kinds of virtuous men worship Me, O Arjuna, and they are the distressed, the seekers of knowledge, the seekers of wealth, and the wise, O Lord of the Bharatas.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_16.mp3]
gita_verse:7.17	<center><big>तेषां ज्ञानी नित्ययुक्त एकभक्ितर्विशिष्यते।<br><br>प्रियो हि ज्ञानिनोऽत्यर्थमहं स च मम प्रियः।।7.17।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>teṣhāṁ jñānī nitya-yukta eka-bhaktir viśhiṣhyate<br>priyo hi jñānino ’tyartham ahaṁ sa cha mama priyaḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Of them, the man of knowledge, endowed with constant steadfastness and one-pointed devotion, excels. gita_verse:7.18	<center><big>उदाराः सर्व एवैते ज्ञानी त्वात्मैव मे मतम्।<br><br>आस्थितः स हि युक्तात्मा मामेवानुत्तमां गतिम्।।7.18।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>udārāḥ sarva evaite jñānī tvātmaiva me matam<br>āsthitaḥ sa hi yuktātmā mām evānuttamāṁ gatim<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Indeed, all of these are noble, but the man of Knowledge is the Self itself. gita_verse:7.19	<center><big>बहूनां जन्मनामन्ते ज्ञानवान्मां प्रपद्यते।<br><br>वासुदेवः सर्वमिति स महात्मा सुदुर्लभः।।7.19।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>bahūnāṁ janmanām ante jñānavān māṁ prapadyate<br>vāsudevaḥ sarvam iti sa mahātmā su-durlabhaḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>At the end of many births, the man of knowledge attains Me, realizing that Vasudeva is all.
