gita_verse:7.20	<center><big>कामैस्तैस्तैर्हृतज्ञानाः प्रपद्यन्तेऽन्यदेवताः।<br><br>तं तं नियममास्थाय प्रकृत्या नियताः स्वया।।7.20।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>kāmais tais tair hṛita-jñānāḥ prapadyante ’nya-devatāḥ<br>taṁ taṁ niyamam āsthāya prakṛityā niyatāḥ svayā<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>People, deprived of their wisdom by desires for various objects and guided by their own nature, resort to other deities, following the relevant methods.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Those whose wisdom has been taken away by this or that desire, go to other gods, following this or that rite, led by their own nature.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_20.mp3]
gita_verse:7.21	<center><big>यो यो यां यां तनुं भक्तः श्रद्धयार्चितुमिच्छति।<br><br>तस्य तस्याचलां श्रद्धां तामेव विदधाम्यहम्।।7.21।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>yo yo yāṁ yāṁ tanuṁ bhaktaḥ śhraddhayārchitum ichchhati<br>tasya tasyāchalāṁ śhraddhāṁ tām eva vidadhāmyaham<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Whichever form of a deity any devotee wants to worship with faith, I strengthen that very firm faith of theirs.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Whatever form any devotee desires to worship with faith, I make that same faith of his firm and unflinching.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_21.mp3]
gita_verse:7.22	<center><big>स तया श्रद्धया युक्तस्तस्याराधनमीहते।<br><br>लभते च ततः कामान्मयैव विहितान् हि तान्।।7.22।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>sa tayā śhraddhayā yuktas tasyārādhanam īhate<br>labhate cha tataḥ kāmān mayaiva vihitān hi tān<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Being imbued with that faith, that person engages in worshipping that form, and they get those very desired results as dispensed by Me alone.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Endowed with that faith, he engages in the worship of that form and obtains his desired outcome, which is ordained by Me alone.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_22.mp3]
gita_verse:7.23	<center><big>अन्तवत्तु फलं तेषां तद्भवत्यल्पमेधसाम्।<br><br>देवान्देवयजो यान्ति मद्भक्ता यान्ति मामपि।।7.23।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>antavat tu phalaṁ teṣhāṁ tad bhavatyalpa-medhasām<br>devān deva-yajo yānti mad-bhaktā yānti mām api<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>The result of those who are of poor intellect is indeed limited. The worshippers of gods go to the gods, while My devotees go to Me alone.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Verily, the reward (fruit) that accrues to those men of small intelligence is finite. The worshippers of the gods go to them, whereas My devotees come to Me.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_23.mp3]
gita_verse:7.24	<center><big>अव्यक्तं व्यक्ितमापन्नं मन्यन्ते मामबुद्धयः।<br><br>परं भावमजानन्तो ममाव्ययमनुत्तमम्।।7.24।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>avyaktaṁ vyaktim āpannaṁ manyante mām abuddhayaḥ<br>paraṁ bhāvam ajānanto mamāvyayam anuttamam<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>The unintelligent, unaware of My supreme state which is immutable and unsurpassable, think of Me as having become manifest from the unmanifest.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>The foolish think of Me, the Unmanifest, as having manifestation, not knowing My higher, immutable, and most excellent nature.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_24.mp3]
gita_verse:7.25	<center><big>नाहं प्रकाशः सर्वस्य योगमायासमावृतः।<br><br>मूढोऽयं नाभिजानाति लोको मामजमव्ययम्।।7.25।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>nāhaṁ prakāśhaḥ sarvasya yoga-māyā-samāvṛitaḥ<br>mūḍho ’yaṁ nābhijānāti loko mām ajam avyayam<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Being enveloped by yoga-maya, I do not become manifest to all. This deluded world does not know Me, who am birthless and undecaying.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>I am not manifest to all, veiled as I am by the Yoga-Maya. This deluded world does not know Me, who am unborn and imperishable.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_25.mp3]
gita_verse:7.26	<center><big>वेदाहं समतीतानि वर्तमानानि चार्जुन।<br><br>भविष्याणि च भूतानि मां तु वेद न कश्चन।।7.26।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>vedāhaṁ samatītāni vartamānāni chārjuna<br>bhaviṣhyāṇi cha bhūtāni māṁ tu veda na kaśhchana<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O Arjuna, I know the past, present, and future beings; but no one knows Me!<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>I know, O Arjuna, the beings of the past, the present, and the future; however, no one knows Me.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_26.mp3]
gita_verse:7.27	<center><big>इच्छाद्वेषसमुत्थेन द्वन्द्वमोहेन भारत।<br><br>सर्वभूतानि संमोहं सर्गे यान्ति परन्तप।।7.27।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>ichchhā-dveṣha-samutthena dvandva-mohena bhārata<br>sarva-bhūtāni sammohaṁ sarge yānti parantapa<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O scion of the Bharata dynasty, O destroyer of foes, due to the delusion of duality arising from likes and dislikes, all creatures become bewildered upon their birth.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>O Bharata, all beings are subject to delusion at birth due to the delusion of the pairs of opposites arising from desire and aversion, O Parantapa.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_27.mp3]
gita_verse:7.28	<center><big>येषां त्वन्तगतं पापं जनानां पुण्यकर्मणाम्।<br><br>ते द्वन्द्वमोहनिर्मुक्ता भजन्ते मां दृढव्रताः।।7.28।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>yeṣhāṁ tvanta-gataṁ pāpaṁ janānāṁ puṇya-karmaṇām<br>te dvandva-moha-nirmuktā bhajante māṁ dṛiḍha-vratāḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>On the other hand, those persons who have done virtuous deeds, whose sin has come to an end, they, being free from the delusion of duality and firm in their convictions, adore Me.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>But those men of virtuous deeds, whose sins have come to an end and who are freed from the delusion of the pairs of opposites, worship Me steadfastly, with their vows.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_28.mp3]
gita_verse:7.29	<center><big>जरामरणमोक्षाय मामाश्रित्य यतन्ति ये।<br><br>ते ब्रह्म तद्विदुः कृत्स्नमध्यात्मं कर्म चाखिलम्।।7.29।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>jarā-maraṇa-mokṣhāya mām āśhritya yatanti ye<br>te brahma tadviduḥ kṛitsnam adhyātmaṁ karma chākhilam<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Those who strive by resorting to Me for becoming free from old age and death, they know Brahman, the individual Self, and all about actions. [They know Brahman as being all the individual entities and all actions. This verse prescribes meditation on the qualified Brahman for aspirants of the middle class. Verses beginning with the 14th speak about the realization of the unqualified Brahman by aspirants of the highest class.]<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Those who strive for liberation from old age and death, taking refuge in Me, realize in full that Brahman, the whole knowledge of the Self, and all action.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_29.mp3]
gita_verse:7.30	<center><big>साधिभूताधिदैवं मां साधियज्ञं च ये विदुः।<br><br>प्रयाणकालेऽपि च मां ते विदुर्युक्तचेतसः।।7.30।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>sādhibhūtādhidaivaṁ māṁ sādhiyajñaṁ cha ye viduḥ<br>prayāṇa-kāle ’pi cha māṁ te vidur yukta-chetasaḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Those who know me as existing in both the physical and divine planes, and also in the context of the sacrifice, they with concentrated minds know me even at the time of death.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Those who know Me with the Adhibhuta (pertaining to the elements), Adhidaiva (pertaining to the gods), and the Adhiyajna (pertaining to the sacrifice) know Me even at the time of death, remaining steadfast in mind.<br><br>[sound:gita_7_30.mp3]
gita_verse:8.1-2	<center><big>अर्जुन उवाच<br><br>किं तद्ब्रह्म किमध्यात्मं किं कर्म पुरुषोत्तम।<br><br>अधिभूतं च किं प्रोक्तमधिदैवं किमुच्यते।।8.1।।<br> <br><br>अधियज्ञः कथं कोऽत्र देहेऽस्मिन्मधुसूदन।<br><br>प्रयाणकाले च कथं ज्ञेयोऽसि नियतात्मभिः।।8.2।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>arjuna uvācha<br>kiṁ tad brahma kim adhyātmaṁ kiṁ karma puruṣhottama<br>adhibhūtaṁ cha kiṁ proktam adhidaivaṁ kim uchyate<br><br>adhiyajñaḥ kathaṁ ko ’tra dehe ’smin madhusūdana<br>prayāṇa-kāle cha kathaṁ jñeyo ’si niyatātmabhiḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Arjuna said, O Supreme Person, what is Brahman? What exists in the individual plane? What is action? What is said to exist in the physical plane? And what is said to exist in the divine plane? O Madhusudana, how is the entity existing in the sacrifice here in this body, and who is it? And how are You to be known by people of concentrated minds at the time of death?<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Arjuna said, "What is Brahman? What is Adhyatma? What is action, O best among men? What is Adhibhuta declared to be? And, what is Adhidaiva said to be?" Who and how is Adhiyajna here in this body, O destroyer of Madhu? And how, at the time of death, are You to be known by the self-controlled?<br><br>[sound:gita_8_1-2.mp3]
gita_verse:8.3	<center><big>श्री भगवानुवाच<br><br>अक्षरं ब्रह्म परमं स्वभावोऽध्यात्ममुच्यते।<br><br>भूतभावोद्भवकरो विसर्गः कर्मसंज्ञितः।।8.3।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>śhrī bhagavān uvācha<br>akṣharaṁ brahma paramaṁ svabhāvo ’dhyātmam uchyate<br>bhūta-bhāvodbhava-karo visargaḥ karma-sanjñitaḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>The Blessed Lord said, "The Immutable is the supreme Brahman; selfhood is said to be the entity present in the individual plane. By action is meant the offerings that bring about the origin of existence of things."<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>The Blessed Lord said, "Brahman is the Imperishable, the Supreme; its essential nature is called Self-knowledge; the offering (to the gods) that causes the existence and manifestation of beings and sustains them is called action."<br><br>[sound:gita_8_3.mp3]
gita_verse:8.4	<center><big>अधिभूतं क्षरो भावः पुरुषश्चाधिदैवतम्।<br><br>अधियज्ञोऽहमेवात्र देहे देहभृतां वर।।8.4।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>adhibhūtaṁ kṣharo bhāvaḥ puruṣhaśh chādhidaivatam<br>adhiyajño ’ham evātra dehe deha-bhṛitāṁ vara<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>That which exists in the physical plane is the mutable entity, and what exists in the divine plane is the Person. O best among the embodied beings, I Myself am the entity that exists in the sacrifice within this body.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Adhibhuta—knowledge of the elements—pertains to My perishable nature, and the Purusha, or the Soul, is the Adhidaiva; I alone am the Adhiyajna here in this body, O best among the embodied.<br><br>[sound:gita_8_4.mp3]
gita_verse:8.5	<center><big>अन्तकाले च मामेव स्मरन्मुक्त्वा कलेवरम्।<br><br>यः प्रयाति स मद्भावं याति नास्त्यत्र संशयः।।8.5।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>anta-kāle cha mām eva smaran muktvā kalevaram<br>yaḥ prayāti sa mad-bhāvaṁ yāti nāstyatra sanśhayaḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>And at the time of death, anyone who departs, giving up the body while thinking of Me alone, attains My state; there is no doubt about this.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>And whoever, leaving their body, goes forth remembering Me alone at the time of death, they will attain My Being; there is no doubt about this.<br><br>[sound:gita_8_5.mp3]
gita_verse:8.6	<center><big>यं यं वापि स्मरन्भावं त्यजत्यन्ते कलेवरम्।<br><br>तं तमेवैति कौन्तेय सदा तद्भावभावितः।।8.6।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>yaṁ yaṁ vāpi smaran bhāvaṁ tyajatyante kalevaram<br>taṁ tam evaiti kaunteya sadā tad-bhāva-bhāvitaḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O son of Kunti, thinking of any entity, whichever it may be, one gives up the body at the end; he attains that very one, having been always engrossed in its thought.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Whoever at the end leaves the body, thinking of any being, to that being only does he go, O son of Kunti (Arjuna), due to his constant thought of that being.<br><br>[sound:gita_8_6.mp3]
gita_verse:8.7	<center><big>तस्मात्सर्वेषु कालेषु मामनुस्मर युध्य च।<br><br>मय्यर्पितमनोबुद्धिर्मामेवैष्यस्यसंशयम्।।8.7।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>tasmāt sarveṣhu kāleṣhu mām anusmara yudhya cha<br>mayyarpita-mano-buddhir mām evaiṣhyasyasanśhayam<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Therefore, think of Me at all times and fight; there is no doubt that by dedicating your mind and intellect to Me, you will attain only Me.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Therefore, at all times, remember Me only and fight. With your mind and intellect fixed on Me, you will undoubtedly come to Me alone.<br><br>[sound:gita_8_7.mp3]
gita_verse:8.8	<center><big>अभ्यासयोगयुक्तेन चेतसा नान्यगामिना।<br><br>परमं पुरुषं दिव्यं याति पार्थानुचिन्तयन्।।8.8।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>abhyāsa-yoga-yuktena chetasā nānya-gāminā<br>paramaṁ puruṣhaṁ divyaṁ yāti pārthānuchintayan<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O son of Prtha, by meditating with a mind engaged in the yoga of practice and not straying away to anything else, one reaches the supreme Person existing in the effulgent region.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>With the mind not moving towards any other thing, made steadfast through the practice of habitual meditation, and constantly meditating, one goes to the Supreme Person, the Resplendent, O Arjuna.<br><br>[sound:gita_8_8.mp3]
gita_verse:8.9-10	<center><big>कविं पुराणमनुशासितार<br><br>मणोरणीयांसमनुस्मरेद्यः।<br><br>सर्वस्य धातारमचिन्त्यरूप<br><br>मादित्यवर्णं तमसः परस्तात्।।8.9।।<br> <br><br>प्रयाणकाले मनसाऽचलेन<br><br>भक्त्या युक्तो योगबलेन चैव।<br><br>भ्रुवोर्मध्ये प्राणमावेश्य सम्यक्<br><br>स तं परं पुरुषमुपैति दिव्यम्।।8.10।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>kaviṁ purāṇam anuśhāsitāram<br>aṇor aṇīyānsam anusmared yaḥ<br>sarvasya dhātāram achintya-rūpam<br>āditya-varṇaṁ tamasaḥ parastāt<br><br>prayāṇa-kāle manasāchalena<br>bhaktyā yukto yoga-balena chaiva<br>bhruvor madhye prāṇam āveśhya samyak<br>sa taṁ paraṁ puruṣham upaiti divyam<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>He who meditates on the Omniscient, the Ancient, the Ruler, subtler than the subtle, the Ordainer of everything, of inconceivable form, effulgent like the sun, and beyond darkness—he attains the Supreme Person. At the time of death, having fully fixed the Prana (vital force) between the eyebrows with an unwavering mind, and being imbued with devotion as well as the strength of concentration, he reaches that resplendent Supreme Person.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Whosoever meditates on the Omniscient, the Ancient, the Ruler of the whole world, minuter than an atom, the supporter of all, of inconceivable form, effulgent like the sun and beyond the darkness of ignorance. At the time of death, with an unwavering mind, endowed with devotion, by the power of Yoga, fixing the whole life-breath in the middle of the two eyebrows, he reaches that resplendent Supreme Person.<br><br>[sound:gita_8_9-10.mp3]
gita_verse:8.11	<center><big>यदक्षरं वेदविदो वदन्ति<br><br>विशन्ति यद्यतयो वीतरागाः।<br><br>यदिच्छन्तो ब्रह्मचर्यं चरन्ति<br><br>तत्ते पदं संग्रहेण प्रवक्ष्ये।।8.11।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>yad akṣharaṁ veda-vido vadanti<br>viśhanti yad yatayo vīta-rāgāḥ<br>yad ichchhanto brahmacharyaṁ charanti<br>tat te padaṁ saṅgraheṇa pravakṣhye<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>I will briefly tell you about that immutable Goal which the knowers of the Vedas declare; those who are diligent, free from attachment, and aspire for it, enter into it. People practice celibacy for it.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>That which is declared to be Imperishable by those who know the Vedas, that which the self-controlled (ascetics or Sannyasins) and passion-free enter, that goal, desiring which celibacy is practised, I will declare to thee in brief.<br><br>[sound:gita_8_11.mp3]
gita_verse:8.12	<center><big>सर्वद्वाराणि संयम्य मनो हृदि निरुध्य च।<br><br>मूर्ध्न्याधायात्मनः प्राणमास्थितो योगधारणाम्।।8.12।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>sarva-dvārāṇi sanyamya mano hṛidi nirudhya cha<br>mūrdhnyādhāyātmanaḥ prāṇam āsthito yoga-dhāraṇām<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Having controlled all the senses, confined the mind in the heart, and fixed his own vital force in the head, he should remain firm in yoga.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Having closed all the gates, confined the mind in the heart, and fixed the life-breath in the head, engage in the practice of concentration.<br><br>[sound:gita_8_12.mp3]
gita_verse:8.13	<center><big>ओमित्येकाक्षरं ब्रह्म व्याहरन्मामनुस्मरन्।<br><br>यः प्रयाति त्यजन्देहं स याति परमां गतिम्।।8.13।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>oṁ ityekākṣharaṁ brahma vyāharan mām anusmaran<br>yaḥ prayāti tyajan dehaṁ sa yāti paramāṁ gatim<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>He who departs, leaving the body while uttering the single syllable, "Om," which is Brahman, and thinking of Me, attains the supreme Goal.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Uttering the one-syllabled Om, the Brahman, and remembering Me, he who departs, leaving the body, attains the Supreme Goal.<br><br>[sound:gita_8_13.mp3]
gita_verse:8.14	<center><big>अनन्यचेताः सततं यो मां स्मरति नित्यशः।<br><br>तस्याहं सुलभः पार्थ नित्ययुक्तस्य योगिनः।।8.14।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>ananya-chetāḥ satataṁ yo māṁ smarati nityaśhaḥ<br>tasyāhaṁ sulabhaḥ pārtha nitya-yuktasya yoginaḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O son of Prtha, to that yogi of constant concentration and single-minded attention, who remembers Me uninterruptedly and for a long time, I am easily attained.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>I am easily attainable by that ever-steadfast yogi who constantly and daily remembers me for a long time, not thinking of anything else with a single-minded or one-pointed focus, O Partha.<br><br>[sound:gita_8_14.mp3]
gita_verse:8.15	<center><big>मामुपेत्य पुनर्जन्म दुःखालयमशाश्वतम्।<br><br>नाप्नुवन्ति महात्मानः संसिद्धिं परमां गताः।।8.15।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>mām upetya punar janma duḥkhālayam aśhāśhvatam<br>nāpnuvanti mahātmānaḥ sansiddhiṁ paramāṁ gatāḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>As a result of reaching Me, the exalted ones who have attained the highest perfection do not get rebirth, which is an abode of sorrows and is impermanent.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Having attained Me, these great souls do not take birth again here—a place of pain and impermanence—but have reached the highest perfection of liberation.<br><br>[sound:gita_8_15.mp3]
gita_verse:8.16	<center><big>आब्रह्मभुवनाल्लोकाः पुनरावर्तिनोऽर्जुन।<br><br>मामुपेत्य तु कौन्तेय पुनर्जन्म न विद्यते।।8.16।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>ā-brahma-bhuvanāl lokāḥ punar āvartino ’rjuna<br>mām upetya tu kaunteya punar janma na vidyate<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O Arjuna, all the worlds together with the world of Brahma are subject to return. But, O son of Kunti, there is no return after reaching Me.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>All the worlds, including the world of Brahma, are subject to return again, O Arjuna; but he who reaches Me, O son of Kunti, has no rebirth.<br><br>[sound:gita_8_16.mp3]
gita_verse:8.17	<center><big>सहस्रयुगपर्यन्तमहर्यद्ब्रह्मणो विदुः।<br><br>रात्रिं युगसहस्रान्तां तेऽहोरात्रविदो जनाः।।8.17।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>sahasra-yuga-paryantam ahar yad brahmaṇo viduḥ<br>rātriṁ yuga-sahasrāntāṁ te ’ho-rātra-vido janāḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Those people who know what day and night are, know the day of Brahma which ends in a thousand yugas, and His night which also ends in a thousand yugas.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Those who know the day of Brahma, which lasts a thousand Yugas, and the night, which also lasts a thousand Yugas, know day and night.<br><br>[sound:gita_8_17.mp3]
gita_verse:8.18	<center><big>अव्यक्ताद्व्यक्तयः सर्वाः प्रभवन्त्यहरागमे।<br><br>रात्र्यागमे प्रलीयन्ते तत्रैवाव्यक्तसंज्ञके।।8.18।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>avyaktād vyaktayaḥ sarvāḥ prabhavantyahar-āgame<br>rātryāgame pralīyante tatraivāvyakta-sanjñake<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>With the coming of day, all manifested things emerge from the Unmanifest, and when night comes, they merge into that which is called the Unmanifested.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>From the Unmanifested, all the manifested worlds proceed upon the arrival of the 'day'; upon the arrival of the 'night', they dissolve indeed into that which is known as the Unmanifested.<br><br>[sound:gita_8_18.mp3]
gita_verse:8.19	<center><big>भूतग्रामः स एवायं भूत्वा भूत्वा प्रलीयते।<br><br>रात्र्यागमेऽवशः पार्थ प्रभवत्यहरागमे।।8.19।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>bhūta-grāmaḥ sa evāyaṁ bhūtvā bhūtvā pralīyate<br>rātryāgame ’vaśhaḥ pārtha prabhavatyahar-āgame<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O son of Prtha, after being born again and again, that very multitude of beings disappears of its own accord at the approach of night. It comes to life again at the approach of day.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>This same multitude of beings, being born again and again, helplessly dissolves, O Arjuna, into the Unmanifested at the coming of the night and comes forth at the coming of the day.<br><br>[sound:gita_8_19.mp3]
gita_verse:8.20	<center><big>परस्तस्मात्तु भावोऽन्योऽव्यक्तोऽव्यक्तात्सनातनः।<br><br>यः स सर्वेषु भूतेषु नश्यत्सु न विनश्यति।।8.20।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>paras tasmāt tu bhāvo ’nyo ’vyakto ’vyaktāt sanātanaḥ<br>yaḥ sa sarveṣhu bhūteṣhu naśhyatsu na vinaśhyati<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>But distinct from that Unmanifested is the other eternal, unmanifest Reality, who does not get destroyed when all beings are destroyed.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>But verily, there exists higher than this Unmanifested, another Unmanifested Eternal, which is not destroyed even when all beings are destroyed.<br><br>[sound:gita_8_20.mp3]
gita_verse:8.21	<center><big>अव्यक्तोऽक्षर इत्युक्तस्तमाहुः परमां गतिम्।<br><br>यं प्राप्य न निवर्तन्ते तद्धाम परमं मम।।8.21।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>avyakto ’kṣhara ityuktas tam āhuḥ paramāṁ gatim<br>yaṁ prāpya na nivartante tad dhāma paramaṁ mama<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>They call Him who has been mentioned as the Unmanifested, the Immutable, the supreme Goal. That is the supreme abode of Mine, from which they do not return once they reach it.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>What is known as the Unmanifested and the Imperishable, That is said to be the highest goal. Those who reach It do not return (to this Samsara). That is My supreme abode (place or state).<br><br>[sound:gita_8_21.mp3]
gita_verse:8.22	<center><big>पुरुषः स परः पार्थ भक्त्या लभ्यस्त्वनन्यया।<br><br>यस्यान्तःस्थानि भूतानि येन सर्वमिदं ततम्।।8.22।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>puruṣhaḥ sa paraḥ pārtha bhaktyā labhyas tvananyayā<br>yasyāntaḥ-sthāni bhūtāni yena sarvam idaṁ tatam<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O son of Prtha, that supreme Person—in whom all beings are included and by whom all this is pervaded—is, indeed, reached through one-pointed devotion.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>That highest Purusha, O Arjuna, is attainable by unswerving devotion to Him alone, within Whom all beings dwell and by Whom all this is pervaded.<br><br>[sound:gita_8_22.mp3]
gita_verse:8.23-26	<center><big>यत्र काले त्वनावृत्तिमावृत्तिं चैव योगिनः।<br><br>प्रयाता यान्ति तं कालं वक्ष्यामि भरतर्षभ।।8.23।।<br> <br><br>अग्निर्ज्योतिरहः शुक्लः षण्मासा उत्तरायणम्।<br><br>तत्र प्रयाता गच्छन्ति ब्रह्म ब्रह्मविदो जनाः।।8.24।।<br> <br><br>धूमो रात्रिस्तथा कृष्णः षण्मासा दक्षिणायनम्।<br><br>तत्र चान्द्रमसं ज्योतिर्योगी प्राप्य निवर्तते।।8.25।।<br> <br><br>शुक्लकृष्णे गती ह्येते जगतः शाश्वते मते।<br><br>एकया यात्यनावृत्तिमन्ययाऽऽवर्तते पुनः।।8.26।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>yatra kāle tvanāvṛittim āvṛittiṁ chaiva yoginaḥ<br>prayātā yānti taṁ kālaṁ vakṣhyāmi bharatarṣhabha<br><br>agnir jyotir ahaḥ śhuklaḥ ṣhaṇ-māsā uttarāyaṇam<br>tatra prayātā gachchhanti brahma brahma-vido janāḥ<br><br>dhūmo rātris tathā kṛiṣhṇaḥ ṣhaṇ-māsā dakṣhiṇāyanam<br>tatra chāndramasaṁ jyotir yogī prāpya nivartate<br><br>śhukla-kṛiṣhṇe gatī hyete jagataḥ śhāśhvate mate<br>ekayā yātyanāvṛittim anyayāvartate punaḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O best of the Bharata dynasty, I shall now speak of that time by which the yogis depart and attain the State of Non-return, and also the State of Return. Fire, light, daytime, the bright fortnight, the six months of the northern solstice—by following this path, persons who are knowers of Brahman attain Brahman when they die. Following this Path, the yogi, having reached the lunar light, returns, smoke, night, as also the dark fortnight and the six months of the Southern solstice. These two paths of the world, which are white and black, are indeed considered eternal. Through one, a person goes to the state of non-return; through the other, they return again.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Now I will tell you, O chief of the Bharatas, the times of departure at which the Yogis will return or not return. Fire, light, daytime, the bright fortnight, the six months of the northern path of the sun (the northern solstice) departing, then men who know Brahman go to Brahman. Attaining the lunar light through smoke, night time, the dark fortnight, and the six months of the southern path of the sun (the southern solstice), the yogi returns. The bright and dark paths of the world are thought to be eternal; one leads to no return, and the other leads to return.<br><br>[sound:gita_8_23-26.mp3]
gita_verse:8.27	<center><big>नैते सृती पार्थ जानन्योगी मुह्यति कश्चन।<br><br>तस्मात्सर्वेषु कालेषु योगयुक्तो भवार्जुन।।8.27।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>naite sṛitī pārtha jānan yogī muhyati kaśhchana<br>tasmāt sarveṣhu kāleṣhu yoga-yukto bhavārjuna<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O son of Prtha, no yogi—one steadfast in meditation—whosoever has known these two courses becomes deluded. Therefore, O Arjuna, be steadfast in yoga at all times.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Knowing these paths, O Arjuna, no yogi is deluded; therefore, at all times, be steadfast in yoga.<br><br>[sound:gita_8_27.mp3]
gita_verse:8.28	<center><big>वेदेषु यज्ञेषु तपःसु चैव<br><br>दानेषु यत्पुण्यफलं प्रदिष्टम्।<br><br>अत्येति तत्सर्वमिदं विदित्वा<br><br>योगी परं स्थानमुपैति चाद्यम्।।8.28।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>vedeṣhu yajñeṣhu tapaḥsu chaiva<br>dāneṣhu yat puṇya-phalaṁ pradiṣhṭam<br>atyeti tat sarvam idaṁ viditvā<br>yogī paraṁ sthānam upaiti chādyam<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Having known this, the yogi transcends all the results of righteous deeds declared in the Vedas, sacrifices, austerities, and charities, and reaches the primordial, supreme state.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Whatever fruit of merit is declared (in the scriptures) to accrue from (the study of) the Vedas, (the performance of) sacrifices, (the practice of) austerities, and gifts, beyond all this goes the Yogi, having known this; and he attains to the Supreme, Primeval (first or ancient) Abode.<br><br>[sound:gita_8_28.mp3]
gita_verse:9.1	<center><big>श्री भगवानुवाच<br><br>इदं तु ते गुह्यतमं प्रवक्ष्याम्यनसूयवे।<br><br>ज्ञानं विज्ञानसहितं यज्ज्ञात्वा मोक्ष्यसेऽशुभात्।।9.1।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>śhrī bhagavān uvācha<br>idaṁ tu te guhyatamaṁ pravakṣhyāmyanasūyave<br>jñānaṁ vijñāna-sahitaṁ yaj jñātvā mokṣhyase ’śhubhāt<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>The Blessed Lord said: However, to you who are not given to cavilling, I shall speak of this highest secret itself, which is knowledge combined with experience, by realizing which you shall be free from evil.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>The Blessed Lord said, "I shall now declare to thee, who does not cavil, the greatest secret—the knowledge combined with experience (Self-realisation). Having known this, thou shalt be free from evil."<br><br>[sound:gita_9_1.mp3]
gita_verse:9.2	<center><big>राजविद्या राजगुह्यं पवित्रमिदमुत्तमम्।<br><br>प्रत्यक्षावगमं धर्म्यं सुसुखं कर्तुमव्ययम्।।9.2।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>rāja-vidyā rāja-guhyaṁ pavitram idam uttamam<br>pratyakṣhāvagamaṁ dharmyaṁ su-sukhaṁ kartum avyayam<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>This is the sovereign knowledge, the sovereign profundity, the best sanctifier; directly realizable, righteous, very easy to practice, and imperishable.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>This is the royal science, the royal secret, the supreme purifier, realizable by direct intuitive knowledge, according to righteousness, very easy to perform and imperishable.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_2.mp3]
gita_verse:9.3	<center><big>अश्रद्दधानाः पुरुषा धर्मस्यास्य परन्तप।<br><br>अप्राप्य मां निवर्तन्ते मृत्युसंसारवर्त्मनि।।9.3।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>aśhraddadhānāḥ puruṣhā dharmasyāsya parantapa<br>aprāpya māṁ nivartante mṛityu-samsāra-vartmani<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O destroyer of foes, those who are disregarding this Dharma (knowledge of the Self) certainly go round and round, without reaching Me, along the path of transmigration which is fraught with death.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Those who have no faith in this Dharma, O Parantapa, return to the path of this world without attaining Me.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_3.mp3]
gita_verse:9.4	<center><big>मया ततमिदं सर्वं जगदव्यक्तमूर्तिना।<br><br>मत्स्थानि सर्वभूतानि न चाहं तेष्ववस्थितः।।9.4।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>mayā tatam idaṁ sarvaṁ jagad avyakta-mūrtinā<br>mat-sthāni sarva-bhūtāni na chāhaṁ teṣhvavasthitaḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>This whole world is pervaded by Me in My unmanifest form. All beings exist in Me, but I am not contained within them!<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>All of this world is pervaded by Me in My unmanifest aspect; all beings exist within Me, but I do not dwell within them.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_4.mp3]
gita_verse:9.5	<center><big>न च मत्स्थानि भूतानि पश्य मे योगमैश्वरम्।<br><br>भूतभृन्न च भूतस्थो ममात्मा भूतभावनः।।9.5।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>na cha mat-sthāni bhūtāni paśhya me yogam aiśhwaram<br>bhūta-bhṛin na cha bhūta-stho mamātmā bhūta-bhāvanaḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Neither do the beings dwell in Me. Behold My divine Yoga! I am the sustainer and originator of beings, but My Self is not contained within the beings.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Nor do beings exist in Me (in reality); behold, My divine Yoga, which supports all beings, but does not dwell in them, is My Self, the efficient cause of beings.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_5.mp3]
gita_verse:9.6	<center><big>यथाऽऽकाशस्थितो नित्यं वायुः सर्वत्रगो महान्।<br><br>तथा सर्वाणि भूतानि मत्स्थानीत्युपधारय।।9.6।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>yathākāśha-sthito nityaṁ vāyuḥ sarvatra-go mahān<br>tathā sarvāṇi bhūtāni mat-sthānītyupadhāraya<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Understand thus that just as the voluminous wind, moving everywhere, is ever present in space, similarly all beings abide in Me.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>As the mighty wind, moving everywhere, always rests in the ether, so too, know that all beings rest in Me.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_6.mp3]
gita_verse:9.7-8	<center><big>सर्वभूतानि कौन्तेय प्रकृतिं यान्ति मामिकाम्।<br><br>कल्पक्षये पुनस्तानि कल्पादौ विसृजाम्यहम्।।9.7।।<br> <br><br>प्रकृतिं स्वामवष्टभ्य विसृजामि पुनः पुनः।<br><br>भूतग्राममिमं कृत्स्नमवशं प्रकृतेर्वशात्।।9.8।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>sarva-bhūtāni kaunteya prakṛitiṁ yānti māmikām<br>kalpa-kṣhaye punas tāni kalpādau visṛijāmyaham<br><br>prakṛitiṁ svām avaṣhṭabhya visṛijāmi punaḥ punaḥ<br>bhūta-grāmam imaṁ kṛitsnam avaśhaṁ prakṛiter vaśhāt<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O son of Kunti, all the beings at the end of a cycle go back to My Prakrti. At the beginning of a cycle, I project them forth again. Keeping My own prakṛti under control, I project forth again and again this multitude of beings, which are powerless due to the influence of their own nature.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>All beings, O Arjuna, go into My Nature at the end of a Kalpa; I send them forth again at the beginning of the next Kalpa. Animating My Nature, I again and again send forth all this multitude of beings, helpless under the force of Nature.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_7-8.mp3]
gita_verse:9.9	<center><big>न च मां तानि कर्माणि निबध्नन्ति धनञ्जय।<br><br>उदासीनवदासीनमसक्तं तेषु कर्मसु।।9.9।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>na cha māṁ tāni karmāṇi nibadhnanti dhanañjaya<br>udāsīna-vad āsīnam asaktaṁ teṣhu karmasu<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O Dhananjaya, those actions do not bind Me, for I remain unconcerned and unattached to them.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>These acts do not bind Me, O Arjuna, sitting as one indifferent, unattached to those acts.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_9.mp3]
gita_verse:9.10	<center><big>मयाऽध्यक्षेण प्रकृतिः सूयते सचराचरम्।<br><br>हेतुनाऽनेन कौन्तेय जगद्विपरिवर्तते।।9.10।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>mayādhyakṣheṇa prakṛitiḥ sūyate sa-charācharam<br>hetunānena kaunteya jagad viparivartate<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Under Me as the supervisor, the Prakrti produces the world of the moving and the non-moving things. Owing to this, O son of Kunti, the world revolves.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Under Me, as supervisor, Nature produces the moving and the unmoving; therefore, O Arjuna, the world revolves.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_10.mp3]
gita_verse:9.11	<center><big>अवजानन्ति मां मूढा मानुषीं तनुमाश्रितम्।<br><br>परं भावमजानन्तो मम भूतमहेश्वरम्।।9.11।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>avajānanti māṁ mūḍhā mānuṣhīṁ tanum āśhritam<br>paraṁ bhāvam ajānanto mama bhūta-maheśhvaram<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Not knowing My supreme nature as the Lord of all beings, foolish people disregard Me, who have taken a human form.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Fools disregard Me, clad in human form, not knowing My higher Being as the great Lord of all beings.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_11.mp3]
gita_verse:9.12	<center><big>मोघाशा मोघकर्माणो मोघज्ञाना विचेतसः।<br><br>राक्षसीमासुरीं चैव प्रकृतिं मोहिनीं श्रिताः।।9.12।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>moghāśhā mogha-karmāṇo mogha-jñānā vichetasaḥ<br>rākṣhasīm āsurīṁ chaiva prakṛitiṁ mohinīṁ śhritāḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Possessed of vain hopes, vain actions, vain knowledge, and senselessness, they become verily possessed of the deceptive disposition of fiends and demons.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>They are possessed of the deceitful nature of demons and undivine beings, filled with vain hopes, vain actions, and vain knowledge that is senseless.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_12.mp3]
gita_verse:9.13	<center><big>महात्मानस्तु मां पार्थ दैवीं प्रकृतिमाश्रिताः।<br><br>भजन्त्यनन्यमनसो ज्ञात्वा भूतादिमव्ययम्।।9.13।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>mahātmānas tu māṁ pārtha daivīṁ prakṛitim āśhritāḥ<br>bhajantyananya-manaso jñātvā bhūtādim avyayam<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O son of Prtha, the noble ones, being possessed of divine nature, surely adore Me with single-mindedness, knowing Me to be the immutable source of all objects.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>But the great souls, O Arjuna, partaking of My divine nature, worship Me with a single-minded devotion, knowing Me as the imperishable source of all beings.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_13.mp3]
gita_verse:9.14	<center><big>सततं कीर्तयन्तो मां यतन्तश्च दृढव्रताः।<br><br>नमस्यन्तश्च मां भक्त्या नित्ययुक्ता उपासते।।9.14।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>satataṁ kīrtayanto māṁ yatantaśh cha dṛiḍha-vratāḥ<br>namasyantaśh cha māṁ bhaktyā nitya-yuktā upāsate<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Always glorifying Me and striving, the men of firm vows worship Me by paying obeisance to Me and being ever endowed with devotion.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Always glorifying Me, striving, firm in their vows, prostrating themselves before Me, they worship Me with steadfast devotion.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_14.mp3]
gita_verse:9.15	<center><big>ज्ञानयज्ञेन चाप्यन्ये यजन्तो मामुपासते।<br><br>एकत्वेन पृथक्त्वेन बहुधा विश्वतोमुखम्।।9.15।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>jñāna-yajñena chāpyanye yajanto mām upāsate<br>ekatvena pṛithaktvena bahudhā viśhvato-mukham<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Others indeed worship Me by exclusively adoring through the sacrifice of the knowledge of oneness; (others worship Me) in many ways, and (others) as the multiform existing in various forms.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Others also, sacrificing with the wisdom-sacrifice, worship Me, the All-Faced, as one, distinct, and manifold.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_15.mp3]
gita_verse:9.16-17	<center><big>अहं क्रतुरहं यज्ञः स्वधाऽहमहमौषधम्।<br><br>मंत्रोऽहमहमेवाज्यमहमग्निरहं हुतम्।।9.16।।<br> <br><br>पिताऽहमस्य जगतो माता धाता पितामहः।<br><br>वेद्यं पवित्रमोंकार ऋक् साम यजुरेव च।।9.17।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>ahaṁ kratur ahaṁ yajñaḥ svadhāham aham auṣhadham<br>mantro ’ham aham evājyam aham agnir ahaṁ hutam<br><br>pitāham asya jagato mātā dhātā pitāmahaḥ<br>vedyaṁ pavitram oṁkāra ṛik sāma yajur eva cha<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>I am the ritual, I am the sacrifice, I am the oblation, I am the medicinal herb, I am the mantra, I am the clarified butter, I am the fire, and I am the act of offering. Of this world, I am the father, mother, ordainer, and grandfather; I am the knowable, the sanctifier, the syllable Om, as well as the Rk, Sama, and Yajus.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>I am Kratu; I am Yajna; I am the offering to the manes; I am the medicinal herbs and all plants; I am the Mantra; I am also the ghee or melted butter; I am the fire; I am the oblation. I am the father of this world, the mother, the dispenser of the fruits of actions, and the grandfather; the one thing to be known, the purifier, the sacred monosyllable (Om), and also the Rik, Sama, and Yajur Vedas.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_16-17.mp3]
gita_verse:9.18	<center><big>गतिर्भर्ता प्रभुः साक्षी निवासः शरणं सुहृत्।<br><br>प्रभवः प्रलयः स्थानं निधानं बीजमव्ययम्।।9.18।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>gatir bhartā prabhuḥ sākṣhī nivāsaḥ śharaṇaṁ suhṛit<br>prabhavaḥ pralayaḥ sthānaṁ nidhānaṁ bījam avyayam<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>I am the fruit of actions, the nourisher, the Lord, witness, abode, refuge, friend, origin, end, foundation, store, and the imperishable seed.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>I am the goal, the supporter, the Lord, the witness, the abode, the shelter, the friend, the origin, the dissolution, the foundation, the treasure-house, and the imperishable seed.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_18.mp3]
gita_verse:9.19	<center><big>तपाम्यहमहं वर्षं निगृह्णाम्युत्सृजामि च।<br><br>अमृतं चैव मृत्युश्च सदसच्चाहमर्जुन।।9.19।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>tapāmyaham ahaṁ varṣhaṁ nigṛihṇāmyutsṛijāmi cha<br>amṛitaṁ chaiva mṛityuśh cha sad asach chāham arjuna<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O Arjuna, I give heat, I withhold and pour down rain; I am verily the nectar, and also death, existence, and non-existence.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>As the sun, I give heat; I withhold and send forth the rain; I am immortality and also death, existence and non-existence, O Arjuna.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_19.mp3]
gita_verse:9.20	<center><big>त्रैविद्या मां सोमपाः पूतपापा<br><br>यज्ञैरिष्ट्वा स्वर्गतिं प्रार्थयन्ते।<br><br>ते पुण्यमासाद्य सुरेन्द्रलोक<br><br>मश्नन्ति दिव्यान्दिवि देवभोगान्।।9.20।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>trai-vidyā māṁ soma-pāḥ pūta-pāpā<br>yajñair iṣhṭvā svar-gatiṁ prārthayante<br>te puṇyam āsādya surendra-lokam<br>aśhnanti divyān divi deva-bhogān<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Those who are versed in the Vedas, who drink Soma and are purified of sin, pray for the heavenly goal by worshipping Me through sacrifices. Having reached the place (world) of the king of gods, which is the result of righteousness, they enjoy the divine pleasure of the gods in heaven.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>The knowers of the three Vedas, the drinkers of Soma, purified of all sins, worshipping Me through sacrifices, pray for the way to heaven; they reach the holy world of the Lord of the gods and enjoy the divine pleasures of the gods in heaven.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_20.mp3]
gita_verse:9.21	<center><big>ते तं भुक्त्वा स्वर्गलोकं विशालं<br><br>क्षीणे पुण्ये मर्त्यलोकं विशन्ति।<br><br>एव त्रयीधर्ममनुप्रपन्ना<br><br>गतागतं कामकामा लभन्ते।।9.21।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>te taṁ bhuktvā swarga-lokaṁ viśhālaṁ<br>kṣhīṇe puṇye martya-lokaṁ viśhanti<br>evaṁ trayī-dharmam anuprapannā<br>gatāgataṁ kāma-kāmā labhante<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>After having enjoyed that vast heavenly world, they enter into the human world upon the exhaustion of their merit. Thus, those who follow the rites and duties prescribed in the three Vedas, and are desirous of pleasures, attain the state of coming and going.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>They, having enjoyed the vast heaven, enter the world of mortals when their merit is exhausted; thus abiding by the injunctions of the three (Vedas) and desiring objects of desires, they attain to the state of coming and going.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_21.mp3]
gita_verse:9.22	<center><big>अनन्याश्चिन्तयन्तो मां ये जनाः पर्युपासते।<br><br>तेषां नित्याभियुक्तानां योगक्षेमं वहाम्यहम्।।9.22।।</big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>ananyāśh chintayanto māṁ ye janāḥ paryupāsate<br>teṣhāṁ nityābhiyuktānāṁ yoga-kṣhemaṁ vahāmyaham<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Those persons who, becoming non-different from Me and meditating, worship Me everywhere, for them, who are ever attached to Me, I arrange for securing what they lack and preserving what they have.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>For those men who worship Me alone, thinking of no one else, for those ever-united, I secure what they have not already possessed and preserve what they already possess.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_22.mp3]
gita_verse:9.23	<center><big>येऽप्यन्यदेवता भक्ता यजन्ते श्रद्धयाऽन्विताः।<br><br>तेऽपि मामेव कौन्तेय यजन्त्यविधिपूर्वकम्।।9.23।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>ye ’pyanya-devatā-bhaktā yajante śhraddhayānvitāḥ<br>te ’pi mām eva kaunteya yajantyavidhi-pūrvakam<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Even those who, being devoted to other deities and endowed with faith, worship them, they also, O son of Kunti, worship Me alone, though following the wrong method.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Even those devotees who, endowed with faith, worship other gods, worship Me alone, O Arjuna, but by the wrong method.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_23.mp3]
gita_verse:9.24	<center><big>अहं हि सर्वयज्ञानां भोक्ता च प्रभुरेव च।<br><br>न तु मामभिजानन्ति तत्त्वेनातश्च्यवन्ति ते।।9.24।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>ahaṁ hi sarva-yajñānāṁ bhoktā cha prabhureva cha<br>na tu mām abhijānanti tattvenātaśh chyavanti te<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Indeed, I am the enjoyer and the Lord of all sacrifices, but they do not know Me truly. Therefore, they fall.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>For I alone am the enjoyer and Lord of all sacrifices; but they do not know Me in reality, and thus they return to this mortal world.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_24.mp3]
gita_verse:9.25	<center><big>यान्ति देवव्रता देवान् पितृ़न्यान्ति पितृव्रताः।<br><br>भूतानि यान्ति भूतेज्या यान्ति मद्याजिनोऽपि माम्।।9.25।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>yānti deva-vratā devān pitṝīn yānti pitṛi-vratāḥ<br>bhūtāni yānti bhūtejyā yānti mad-yājino ’pi mām<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Those who worship the gods reach the gods; the worshippers of the manes go to the manes; the devotees of the Beings reach the Beings; and those who worship Me come to Me.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>The worshippers of the gods go to them; the ancestor-worshippers go to the manes; the worshippers of the deities who preside over the elements go to them; but My devotees come to Me.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_25.mp3]
gita_verse:9.26	<center><big>पत्रं पुष्पं फलं तोयं यो मे भक्त्या प्रयच्छति।<br><br>तदहं भक्त्युपहृतमश्नामि प्रयतात्मनः।।9.26।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>patraṁ puṣhpaṁ phalaṁ toyaṁ yo me bhaktyā prayachchhati<br>tadahaṁ bhaktyupahṛitam aśhnāmi prayatātmanaḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Whoever offers Me with devotion—a leaf, a flower, a fruit, or water—I accept that gift of the pure-hearted man which has been presented devotionally.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Whoever offers Me with devotion a leaf, a flower, a fruit, or a little water, that, so offered devotedly by the pure-minded, I accept.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_26.mp3]
gita_verse:9.27	<center><big>यत्करोषि यदश्नासि यज्जुहोषि ददासि यत्।<br><br>यत्तपस्यसि कौन्तेय तत्कुरुष्व मदर्पणम्।।9.27।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>yat karoṣhi yad aśhnāsi yaj juhoṣhi dadāsi yat<br>yat tapasyasi kaunteya tat kuruṣhva mad-arpaṇam<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O son of Kunti, whatever you do, whatever you eat, whatever you offer as a sacrifice, whatever you give, and whatever austerities you undertake—all of that you offer to Me.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Whatever you do, whatever you eat, whatever you offer in sacrifice, whatever you give, whatever austerity you practice, O Arjuna, do it as an offering to Me.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_27.mp3]
gita_verse:9.28	<center><big>शुभाशुभफलैरेवं मोक्ष्यसे कर्मबन्धनैः।<br><br>संन्यासयोगयुक्तात्मा विमुक्तो मामुपैष्यसि।।9.28।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>śhubhāśhubha-phalair evaṁ mokṣhyase karma-bandhanaiḥ<br>sannyāsa-yoga-yuktātmā vimukto mām upaiṣhyasi<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Thus, you will become free from bondage in the form of actions which are productive of good and bad results. Having your mind imbued with the yoga of renunciation and becoming free, you will attain Me.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Thus, you shall be freed from the bonds of actions yielding good and evil fruits; with the mind steadfast in the Yoga of renunciation, and liberated, you shall come to Me.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_28.mp3]
gita_verse:9.29	<center><big>समोऽहं सर्वभूतेषु न मे द्वेष्योऽस्ति न प्रियः।<br><br>ये भजन्ति तु मां भक्त्या मयि ते तेषु चाप्यहम्।।9.29।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>samo ’haṁ sarva-bhūteṣhu na me dveṣhyo ’sti na priyaḥ<br>ye bhajanti tu māṁ bhaktyā mayi te teṣhu chāpyaham<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>I am impartial towards all beings; to Me there is none detestable or none dear. But those who worship Me with devotion, they exist in Me, and I too exist in them.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>I am the same to all beings; there is none hateful or dear to Me; but those who worship Me with devotion are in Me, and I am also in them.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_29.mp3]
gita_verse:9.30	<center><big>अपि चेत्सुदुराचारो भजते मामनन्यभाक्।<br><br>साधुरेव स मन्तव्यः सम्यग्व्यवसितो हि सः।।9.30।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>api chet su-durāchāro bhajate mām ananya-bhāk<br>sādhur eva sa mantavyaḥ samyag vyavasito hi saḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Even if a man of very bad conduct worships Me with single-minded devotion, he is to be considered truly good; for he has rightly resolved.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Even if the most sinful worships Me, with devotion to no one else, he should indeed be regarded as righteous, for he has rightly resolved.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_30.mp3]
gita_verse:9.31	<center><big>क्षिप्रं भवति धर्मात्मा शश्वच्छान्तिं निगच्छति।<br><br>कौन्तेय प्रतिजानीहि न मे भक्तः प्रणश्यति।।9.31।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>kṣhipraṁ bhavati dharmātmā śhaśhvach-chhāntiṁ nigachchhati<br>kaunteya pratijānīhi na me bhaktaḥ praṇaśhyati<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>He soon becomes possessed of a virtuous mind; he attains everlasting peace. Do you proclaim boldly, O son of Kunti, that My devotee will not be ruined.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Soon he becomes righteous and attains eternal peace; O Arjuna, proclaim thou for certain that My devotee never perishes.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_31.mp3]
gita_verse:9.32	<center><big>मां हि पार्थ व्यपाश्रित्य येऽपि स्युः पापयोनयः।<br><br>स्त्रियो वैश्यास्तथा शूद्रास्तेऽपि यान्ति परां गतिम्।।9.32।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>māṁ hi pārtha vyapāśhritya ye ’pi syuḥ pāpa-yonayaḥ<br>striyo vaiśhyās tathā śhūdrās te ’pi yānti parāṁ gatim<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>For, O son of Prtha, even those who are born of sin-women, Vaisyas, as well as Sudras—[S.'s construction of this portion is: women, Vaisyas as well as Sudras, and even others who are born of sin (i.e., those who are born low and are of vile deeds, viz Mlecchas, Pukkasas and others). M.S. also takes papa-yonayah (born of sin) as a separate phrase, and classifies women and others only as those darred from Vedic study, etc.-Tr.]—even they reach the highest Goal by taking shelter under Me.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>For, taking refuge in Me, they who, O Arjuna, may be of a sinful birth—women, Vaisyas, and Sudras—attain the Supreme Goal.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_32.mp3]
gita_verse:9.33	<center><big>किं पुनर्ब्राह्मणाः पुण्या भक्ता राजर्षयस्तथा।<br><br>अनित्यमसुखं लोकमिमं प्राप्य भजस्व माम्।।9.33।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>kiṁ punar brāhmaṇāḥ puṇyā bhaktā rājarṣhayas tathā<br>anityam asukhaṁ lokam imaṁ prāpya bhajasva mām<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>What of the holy Brahmanas and devoted, wise sages? Having come to this fleeting, miserable world, worship Me.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>How much more easily, then, do Brahmins and devoted royal saints attain the goal? Having come to this impermanent and unhappy world, do thou worship Me.<br><br>[sound:gita_9_33.mp3]

gita_verse:11.4	<center><big>मन्यसे यदि तच्छक्यं मया द्रष्टुमिति प्रभो।<br><br>योगेश्वर ततो मे त्वं दर्शयाऽत्मानमव्ययम्।।11.4।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>manyase yadi tach chhakyaṁ mayā draṣhṭum iti prabho<br>yogeśhvara tato me tvaṁ darśhayātmānam avyayam<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O Lord, if You deem it possible for me to behold You, then, O Lord of Yoga, show me Your eternal Self.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>If Thou, O Lord, thinkest it possible for me to see it, do Thou, then, O Lord of the Yogis, show me Thy imperishable Self.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_4.mp3]
gita_verse:11.5	<center><big>श्री भगवानुवाच<br><br>पश्य मे पार्थ रूपाणि शतशोऽथ सहस्रशः।<br><br>नानाविधानि दिव्यानि नानावर्णाकृतीनि च।।11.5।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>śhrī-bhagavān uvācha<br>paśhya me pārtha rūpāṇi śhataśho ’tha sahasraśhaḥ<br>nānā-vidhāni divyāni nānā-varṇākṛitīni cha<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>The Blessed Lord said, "O son of Prtha, behold My forms in their hundreds and thousands, of different kinds, celestial, and of various colors and shapes."<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>The Blessed Lord said, "Behold, O Arjuna, forms of Mine, by the hundreds and thousands, of different sorts, divine, and of various colors and shapes."<br><br>[sound:gita_11_5.mp3]
gita_verse:11.6	<center><big>पश्यादित्यान्वसून्रुद्रानश्िवनौ मरुतस्तथा।<br><br>बहून्यदृष्टपूर्वाणि पश्याऽश्चर्याणि भारत।।11.6।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>paśhyādityān vasūn rudrān aśhvinau marutas tathā<br>bahūny adṛiṣhṭa-pūrvāṇi paśhyāśhcharyāṇi bhārata<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Behold the Adityas, the Vasus, the Rudras, the two Ashvins, and the Maruts. O scion of the Bharata dynasty, also behold the many wonders that have never been seen before.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Behold the Adityas, the Vasus, the Rudras, the two Asvins, and the Maruts; behold many wonders never before seen, O Arjuna.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_6.mp3]
gita_verse:11.7	<center><big>इहैकस्थं जगत्कृत्स्नं पश्याद्य सचराचरम्।<br><br>मम देहे गुडाकेश यच्चान्यद्द्रष्टुमिच्छसि।।11.7।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>ihaika-sthaṁ jagat kṛitsnaṁ paśhyādya sa-charācharam<br>mama dehe guḍākeśha yach chānyad draṣhṭum ichchhasi<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>See now, O Gudakesa, the entire Universe together with the moving and the non-moving, concentrated in the same place here in My body, as also whatever else you would like to see.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Now, behold, O Arjuna, in this My body, the entire universe centered in one, including the moving and the unmoving, and whatever else you desire to see.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_7.mp3]
gita_verse:11.8	<center><big>न तु मां शक्यसे द्रष्टुमनेनैव स्वचक्षुषा।<br><br>दिव्यं ददामि ते चक्षुः पश्य मे योगमैश्वरम्।।11.8।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>na tu māṁ śhakyase draṣhṭum anenaiva sva-chakṣhuṣhā<br>divyaṁ dadāmi te chakṣhuḥ paśhya me yogam aiśhwaram<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>But you are not able to see Me with just this eye of yours. I grant you the divine eye; behold My divine Yoga.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>But you are not able to behold Me with these your own eyes; I give you the divine eye; behold My lordly Yoga.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_8.mp3]
gita_verse:11.9	<center><big>सञ्जय उवाच<br><br>एवमुक्त्वा ततो राजन्महायोगेश्वरो हरिः।<br><br>दर्शयामास पार्थाय परमं रूपमैश्वरम्।।11.9।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>sañjaya uvācha<br>evam uktvā tato rājan mahā-yogeśhvaro hariḥ<br>darśhayām āsa pārthāya paramaṁ rūpam aiśhwaram<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Sanjaya said, "O King, having spoken thus, thereafter, Hari, the great Master of Yoga, showed to the son of Prtha the supreme divine form."<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Sanjaya said, Having thus spoken, O king, the great Lord of Yoga, Hari (Krishna), showed Arjuna His supreme form as the Lord.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_9.mp3]
gita_verse:11.10-11	<center><big>अनेकवक्त्रनयनमनेकाद्भुतदर्शनम्।<br><br>अनेकदिव्याभरणं दिव्यानेकोद्यतायुधम्।।11.10।।<br> <br><br>दिव्यमाल्याम्बरधरं दिव्यगन्धानुलेपनम्।<br><br>सर्वाश्चर्यमयं देवमनन्तं विश्वतोमुखम्।।11.11।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>aneka-vaktra-nayanam anekādbhuta-darśhanam<br>aneka-divyābharaṇaṁ divyānekodyatāyudham<br><br>divya-mālyāmbara-dharaṁ divya-gandhānulepanam<br>sarvāśhcharya-mayaṁ devam anantaṁ viśhvato-mukham<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Having many faces and eyes, possessing many wondrous sights, adorned with numerous celestial ornaments, and holding many uplifted heavenly weapons; Wearing heavenly garlands and apparel, anointed with heavenly scents, abounding in all kinds of wonders, resplendent, infinite, and with faces on all sides.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>With numerous mouths and eyes, with numerous wondrous sights, with numerous divine adornments, with numerous divine weapons uplifted, such a form He showed. Wearing divine garlands and apparel, anointed with divine unguents, the all-wonderful, resplendent Being is endless with faces on all sides.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_10-11.mp3]
gita_verse:11.12	<center><big>दिवि सूर्यसहस्रस्य भवेद्युगपदुत्थिता।<br><br>यदि भाः सदृशी सा स्याद्भासस्तस्य महात्मनः।।11.12।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>divi sūrya-sahasrasya bhaved yugapad utthitā<br>yadi bhāḥ sadṛiśhī sā syād bhāsas tasya mahātmanaḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Should the effulgence of a thousand suns blaze forth simultaneously in the sky, that might be akin to the radiance of that exalted One.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>If the splendour of a thousand suns were to blaze out simultaneously in the sky, that would be the splendour of that mighty being.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_12.mp3]
gita_verse:11.13	<center><big>तत्रैकस्थं जगत्कृत्स्नं प्रविभक्तमनेकधा।<br><br>अपश्यद्देवदेवस्य शरीरे पाण्डवस्तदा।।11.13।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>tatraika-sthaṁ jagat kṛitsnaṁ pravibhaktam anekadhā<br>apaśhyad deva-devasya śharīre pāṇḍavas tadā<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>At that time, the Pandava saw, in the body of the God of gods, the whole diversely differentiated universe united in one.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>There, in the body of the God of gods, Arjuna then saw the entire universe resting in one, with its myriad of divisions.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_13.mp3]
gita_verse:11.14	<center><big>ततः स विस्मयाविष्टो हृष्टरोमा धनञ्जयः।<br><br>प्रणम्य शिरसा देवं कृताञ्जलिरभाषत।।11.14।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>tataḥ sa vismayāviṣhṭo hṛiṣhṭa-romā dhanañjayaḥ<br>praṇamya śhirasā devaṁ kṛitāñjalir abhāṣhata<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Then, filled with wonder and with hairs standing on end, Arjuna, bowing down with his head to the Lord, said with folded hands:<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Then, Arjuna, filled with wonder and his hair standing on end, bowed his head to the God and spoke with palms joined.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_14.mp3]
gita_verse:11.15	<center><big>अर्जुन उवाच<br><br>पश्यामि देवांस्तव देव देहे<br><br>सर्वांस्तथा भूतविशेषसङ्घान्।<br><br>ब्रह्माणमीशं कमलासनस्थ<br><br>मृषींश्च सर्वानुरगांश्च दिव्यान्।।11.15।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>arjuna uvācha<br>paśhyāmi devāns tava deva dehe<br>sarvāns tathā bhūta-viśheṣha-saṅghān<br>brahmāṇam īśhaṁ kamalāsana-stham<br>ṛiṣhīnśh cha sarvān uragānśh cha divyān<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Arjuna said, "O God, I see in Your body all the gods, as well as hosts of various classes of beings; Brahma the ruler, sitting on a lotus seat, and all the heavenly sages and serpents.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Arjuna said, "O God, I see all the gods in Your body, as well as hosts of various classes of beings, Brahma the Lord seated on the lotus, all the sages, and the celestial serpents."<br><br>[sound:gita_11_15.mp3]
gita_verse:11.16	<center><big>अनेकबाहूदरवक्त्रनेत्रं<br><br>पश्यामि त्वां सर्वतोऽनन्तरूपम्।<br><br>नान्तं न मध्यं न पुनस्तवादिं<br><br>पश्यामि विश्वेश्वर विश्वरूप।।11.16।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>aneka-bāhūdara-vaktra-netraṁ<br>paśhyāmi tvāṁ sarvato ’nanta-rūpam<br>nāntaṁ na madhyaṁ na punas tavādiṁ<br>paśhyāmi viśhveśhvara viśhva-rūpa<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>I see You with numerous arms, bellies, mouths, and eyes; with infinite forms all around. O Lord of the Universe, O Cosmic Person, I see no limit, no middle, nor beginning!<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>I see You with boundless form on every side, with many arms, stomachs, mouths, and eyes; neither the end nor the middle nor the beginning do I see, O Lord of the Universe, O Cosmic Form.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_16.mp3]
gita_verse:11.17	<center><big>किरीटिनं गदिनं चक्रिणं च<br><br>तेजोराशिं सर्वतोदीप्तिमन्तम्।<br><br>पश्यामि त्वां दुर्निरीक्ष्यं समन्ता<br><br>द्दीप्तानलार्कद्युतिमप्रमेयम्।।11.17।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>kirīṭinaṁ gadinaṁ chakriṇaṁ cha<br>tejo-rāśhiṁ sarvato dīptimantam<br>paśhyāmi tvāṁ durnirīkṣhyaṁ samantād<br>dīptānalārka-dyutim aprameyam<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>I see You wearing a diadem, wielding a mace, and holding a disc; a mass of brilliance glowing all around, difficult to look at from all sides, possessing the radiance of the blazing fire and sun, and immeasurable.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>I see You with the diadem, club, and discus, a mass of radiance shining everywhere, very hard to look at, blazing all around like a burning fire and the sun, and immeasurable.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_17.mp3]
gita_verse:11.18	<center><big>त्वमक्षरं परमं वेदितव्यं<br><br>त्वमस्य विश्वस्य परं निधानम्।<br><br>त्वमव्ययः शाश्वतधर्मगोप्ता<br><br>सनातनस्त्वं पुरुषो मतो मे।।11.18।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>tvam akṣharaṁ paramaṁ veditavyaṁ<br>tvam asya viśhvasya paraṁ nidhānam<br>tvam avyayaḥ śhāśhvata-dharma-goptā<br>sanātanas tvaṁ puruṣho mato me<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>You are the Unchanging, the supreme One to be known; You are the most perfect repository of this Universe. You are the Imperishable, the Protector of the ever-existing religion; You are the eternal Person. This is my belief.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>You are the Imperishable, the Supreme Being, worthy of being known. You are the great treasure-house of this universe; You are the imperishable protector of the eternal Dharma; You are the Primal Person, I believe.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_18.mp3]
gita_verse:11.19	<center><big>अनादिमध्यान्तमनन्तवीर्य<br><br>मनन्तबाहुं शशिसूर्यनेत्रम्।<br><br>पश्यामि त्वां दीप्तहुताशवक्त्रम्<br><br>स्वतेजसा विश्वमिदं तपन्तम्।।11.19।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>स्वतेजसा विश्वमिदं तपन्तम् || 19||<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>I see You as having no beginning, middle, or end, possessing infinite valor, with innumerable arms, the sun and moon as eyes, a mouth like a blazing fire, and heating up this universe with Your own brilliance.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>I see You without beginning, middle, or end, infinite in power, with endless arms, the sun and moon as Your eyes, the burning fire Your mouth, heating the entire universe with Your radiance.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_19.mp3]
gita_verse:11.20	<center><big>द्यावापृथिव्योरिदमन्तरं हि<br><br>व्याप्तं त्वयैकेन दिशश्च सर्वाः।<br><br>दृष्ट्वाऽद्भुतं रूपमुग्रं तवेदं<br><br>लोकत्रयं प्रव्यथितं महात्मन्।।11.20।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>dyāv ā-pṛithivyor idam antaraṁ hi<br>vyāptaṁ tvayaikena diśhaśh cha sarvāḥ<br>dṛiṣhṭvādbhutaṁ rūpam ugraṁ tavedaṁ<br>loka-trayaṁ pravyathitaṁ mahātman<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Indeed, this intermediate space between heaven and earth, as well as all the directions, are pervaded by You alone. O exalted One, the three worlds are struck with fear upon seeing this strange and fearful form of Yours.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>This space between the earth and the heavens, and all the quarters, is filled by You alone; having seen this, Your wonderful and terrible form, the three worlds are trembling with fear, O great-souled Being.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_20.mp3]
gita_verse:11.21	<center><big>अमी हि त्वां सुरसङ्घाः विशन्ति<br><br>केचिद्भीताः प्राञ्जलयो गृणन्ति।<br><br>स्वस्तीत्युक्त्वा महर्षिसिद्धसङ्घाः<br><br>स्तुवन्ति त्वां स्तुतिभिः पुष्कलाभिः।।11.21।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>amī hi tvāṁ sura-saṅghā viśhanti<br>kechid bhītāḥ prāñjalayo gṛiṇanti<br>svastīty uktvā maharṣhi-siddha-saṅghāḥ<br>stuvanti tvāṁ stutibhiḥ puṣhkalābhiḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Those very groups of gods enter into You; struck with fear, some extol You with joined palms. Groups of great sages and perfected beings praise You with elaborate hymns, saying, 'May it be well!'<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Verily, these hosts of gods enter into Thee; some extol Thee with joined palms in fear, saying, 'May it be well!' Bands of great sages and perfected ones praise Thee with complete hymns.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_21.mp3]
gita_verse:11.22	<center><big>रुद्रादित्या वसवो ये च साध्या<br><br>विश्वेऽश्िवनौ मरुतश्चोष्मपाश्च।<br><br>गन्धर्वयक्षासुरसिद्धसङ्घा<br><br>वीक्षन्ते त्वां विस्मिताश्चैव सर्वे।।11.22।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>rudrādityā vasavo ye cha sādhyā<br>viśhve ’śhvinau marutaśh choṣhmapāśh cha<br>gandharva-yakṣhāsura-siddha-saṅghā<br>vīkṣhante tvāṁ vismitāśh chaiva sarve<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Those who are the Rudras, the Adityas, the Vasus, and the Sadhyas, the Visvedevas, the two Asvins, the Maruts, and the Usmapas, and hosts of Gandharvas, Yaksas, demons, and Siddhas—all of those very ones gaze at You, being indeed struck with wonder.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>The Rudras, Adityas, Vasus, Sadhyas, Visvedevas, the two Asvins, Maruts, the Manus, and the hosts of celestial singers, Yakshas, demons, and the perfected ones, all look upon Thee with great amazement.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_22.mp3]
gita_verse:11.23	<center><big>रूपं महत्ते बहुवक्त्रनेत्रं<br><br>महाबाहो बहुबाहूरुपादम्।<br><br>बहूदरं बहुदंष्ट्राकरालं<br><br>दृष्ट्वा लोकाः प्रव्यथितास्तथाऽहम्।।11.23।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>rūpaṁ mahat te bahu-vaktra-netraṁ<br>mahā-bāho bahu-bāhūru-pādam<br>bahūdaraṁ bahu-danṣhṭrā-karālaṁ<br>dṛiṣhṭvā lokāḥ pravyathitās tathāham<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O Mighty-Armed One, seeing Your immense form with many mouths, eyes, arms, thighs, feet, bellies, and teeth, the creatures are struck with terror, and so am I.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Having seen Your immeasurable form with many mouths and eyes, O mighty-armed one, with many arms, thighs, and feet, with many stomachs and fearsome with many teeth, the worlds are terrified, and so am I.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_23.mp3]
gita_verse:11.24	<center><big>नभःस्पृशं दीप्तमनेकवर्णं<br><br>व्यात्ताननं दीप्तविशालनेत्रम्।<br><br>दृष्ट्वा हि त्वां प्रव्यथितान्तरात्मा<br><br>धृतिं न विन्दामि शमं च विष्णो।।11.24।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>nabhaḥ-spṛiśhaṁ dīptam aneka-varṇaṁ<br>vyāttānanaṁ dīpta-viśhāla-netram<br>dṛiṣhṭvā hi tvāṁ pravyathitāntar-ātmā<br>dhṛitiṁ na vindāmi śhamaṁ cha viṣhṇo<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>O Vishnu, indeed, upon seeing Your form touching the heavens, blazing with many colors, open-mouthed, with fiery, large eyes, I become terrified in my mind and do not find steadiness and peace.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>On seeing Thee, touching the sky, shining in many colors, with mouths wide open, with large fiery eyes, I am terrified at heart and find neither courage nor peace, O Vishnu.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_24.mp3]
gita_verse:11.25	<center><big>दंष्ट्राकरालानि च ते मुखानि<br><br>दृष्ट्वैव कालानलसन्निभानि।<br><br>दिशो न जाने न लभे च शर्म<br><br>प्रसीद देवेश जगन्निवास।।11.25।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>danṣhṭrā-karālāni cha te mukhāni<br>dṛiṣhṭvaiva kālānala-sannibhāni<br>diśho na jāne na labhe cha śharma<br>prasīda deveśha jagan-nivāsa<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Having merely seen Your mouths made terrible with their teeth and resembling the fire of Dissolution, I have lost my sense of direction and find no comfort. Be gracious, O Lord of gods, O Abode of the Universe.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Having seen Thy mouths fearful with teeth blazing like the fires of cosmic dissolution, I know not the four quarters, nor do I find peace. Have mercy, O Lord of the gods, O abode of the universe.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_25.mp3]

They rapidly enter into Your terrible mouths with cruel teeth! Some are seen sticking in the gaps between the teeth, with their heads crushed!<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>All the sons of Dhritarashtra, along with the hosts of kings of the earth, Bhishma, Drona, and Karna, as well as the chief among our warriors. Some hurry into Your mouths with their terrible teeth, fearful to behold. Some are found stuck in the gaps between the teeth, their heads crushed to powder.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_26-27.mp3]
gita_verse:11.28-29	<center><big>यथा नदीनां बहवोऽम्बुवेगाः<br><br>समुद्रमेवाभिमुखाः द्रवन्ति।<br><br>तथा तवामी नरलोकवीरा<br><br>विशन्ति वक्त्राण्यभिविज्वलन्ति।।11.28।।<br> <br><br>यथा प्रदीप्तं ज्वलनं पतङ्गा<br><br>विशन्ति नाशाय समृद्धवेगाः।<br><br>तथैव नाशाय विशन्ति लोका<br><br>स्तवापि वक्त्राणि समृद्धवेगाः।।11.29।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>yathā nadīnāṁ bahavo ’mbu-vegāḥ<br>samudram evābhimukhā dravanti<br>tathā tavāmī nara-loka-vīrā<br>viśhanti vaktrāṇy abhivijvalanti<br><br>yathā pradīptaṁ jvalanaṁ pataṅgā<br>viśhanti nāśhāya samṛiddha-vegāḥ<br>tathaiva nāśhāya viśhanti lokās<br>tavāpi vaktrāṇi samṛiddha-vegāḥ<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>As the numerous currents of the waters of rivers rush towards the sea alone, so too do those heroes of the human world enter into Your blazing mouths. As moths hasten with increased speed into a blazing fire for destruction, so too do creatures hasten into Your mouths with increased speed for destruction.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Verily, just as many torrents of rivers flow towards the ocean, so too these heroes in the world of men enter Thy flaming mouths. As moths hurriedly rush into a blazing fire, leading to their own destruction, so too these creatures hurry into Your mouths, leading to their own destruction.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_28-29.mp3]

gita_verse:11.35	<center><big>सञ्जय उवाच<br><br>एतच्छ्रुत्वा वचनं केशवस्य<br><br>कृताञ्जलिर्वेपमानः किरीटी।<br><br>नमस्कृत्वा भूय एवाह कृष्णं<br><br>सगद्गदं भीतभीतः प्रणम्य।।11.35।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>sañjaya uvācha<br>etach chhrutvā vachanaṁ keśhavasya<br>kṛitāñjalir vepamānaḥ kirīṭī<br>namaskṛitvā bhūya evāha kṛiṣhṇaṁ<br>sa-gadgadaṁ bhīta-bhītaḥ praṇamya<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Sanjaya said: Hearing this utterance of Kesava, Kiriti (Arjuna), with joined palms and trembling, prostrated himself, and then, with a faltering voice, bowed down and overcome by fits of fear, said again to Krsna:<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Sanjaya said, Having heard that speech of Lord Krishna, Arjuna, with joined palms, trembling, prostrated himself, again addressing Krishna in a choked voice, bowing down, overwhelmed with fear.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_35.mp3]

gita_verse:11.41-42	<center><big>सखेति मत्वा प्रसभं यदुक्तं<br><br>हे कृष्ण हे यादव हे सखेति।<br><br>अजानता महिमानं तवेदं<br><br>मया प्रमादात्प्रणयेन वापि।।11.41।।<br> <br><br>यच्चावहासार्थमसत्कृतोऽसि<br><br>विहारशय्यासनभोजनेषु।<br><br>एकोऽथवाप्यच्युत तत्समक्षं<br><br>तत्क्षामये त्वामहमप्रमेयम्।।11.42।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>sakheti matvā prasabhaṁ yad uktaṁ<br>he kṛiṣhṇa he yādava he sakheti<br>ajānatā mahimānaṁ tavedaṁ<br>mayā pramādāt praṇayena vāpi<br><br>yach chāvahāsārtham asat-kṛito ’si<br>vihāra-śhayyāsana-bhojaneṣhu<br>eko ’tha vāpy achyuta tat-samakṣhaṁ<br>tat kṣhāmaye tvām aham aprameyam<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Without knowing Your greatness, whatever I said rashly, inadvertently, or even out of familiarity, thinking You to be a friend, addressing You as 'O Krsna,' 'O Yadava,' 'O friend,' etc. And that You have been discourteously treated out of fun—while walking, while on a bed, while on a seat, while eating, in privacy, or, O Acyuta, even in public—for that, I beg pardon of You, the incomprehensible One.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Whatever I have presumptuously said from carelessness or love, addressing You as O Krishna! O Yadava! O Friend! regarding You merely as a friend, unknowing of Your greatness. In whatever way I may have insulted You for the sake of fun, while at play, reposing, sitting, or at meals, when alone (with You), O Krishna, or in company, that I implore You, immeasurable one, to forgive.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_41-42.mp3]
gita_verse:11.43	<center><big>पितासि लोकस्य चराचरस्य<br><br>त्वमस्य पूज्यश्च गुरुर्गरीयान्।<br><br>न त्वत्समोऽस्त्यभ्यधिकः कुतोऽन्यो<br><br>लोकत्रयेऽप्यप्रतिमप्रभाव।।11.43।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>pitāsi lokasya charācharasya<br>tvam asya pūjyaśh cha gurur garīyān<br>na tvat-samo ’sty abhyadhikaḥ kuto ’nyo<br>loka-traye ’py apratima-prabhāva<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>You are the Father of all beings, both moving and non-moving; to You, the Teacher, are they worthy of worship, and You are greater than a teacher. There is none equal to You; how can there be anyone greater even in all the three worlds, O You of unrivaled power?<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Thou art the Father of this world, both moving and unmoving. Thou art to be adored by this world; Thou, the greatest Guru; for none exists who is equal to Thee; how then could there be another superior to Thee in the three worlds, O Being of unrivaled power?<br><br>[sound:gita_11_43.mp3]
gita_verse:11.44	<center><big>तस्मात्प्रणम्य प्रणिधाय कायं<br><br>प्रसादये त्वामहमीशमीड्यम्।<br><br>पितेव पुत्रस्य सखेव सख्युः<br><br>प्रियः प्रियायार्हसि देव सोढुम्।।11.44।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>tasmāt praṇamya praṇidhāya kāyaṁ<br>prasādaye tvām aham īśham īḍyam<br>piteva putrasya sakheva sakhyuḥ<br>priyaḥ priyāyārhasi deva soḍhum<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Therefore, by bowing down and prostrating my body, I seek to propitiate You who are God and are adorable. O Lord, You should forgive my faults as a father would forgive the faults of a son, as a friend would forgive the faults of a friend, and as a lover would forgive the faults of a beloved.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Therefore, bowing down and prostrating my body, I crave Thy forgiveness, O adorable Lord. As a father forgives his son, a friend his dear friend, a lover his beloved, even so may Thou forgive me, O God.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_44.mp3]
gita_verse:11.45	<center><big>अदृष्टपूर्वं हृषितोऽस्मि दृष्ट्वा<br><br>भयेन च प्रव्यथितं मनो मे।<br><br>तदेव मे दर्शय देव रूपं<br><br>प्रसीद देवेश जगन्निवास।।11.45।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>adṛiṣhṭa-pūrvaṁ hṛiṣhito ’smi dṛiṣhṭvā<br>bhayena cha pravyathitaṁ mano me<br>tad eva me darśhaya deva rūpaṁ<br>prasīda deveśha jagan-nivāsa<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>I am delighted by seeing something I have not seen before, and my mind is stricken with fear. O Lord, show me that very form; O Supreme God, O Abode of the Universe, be gracious!<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>I am delighted, having seen something never seen before; yet my mind is distressed with fear. Show me that form only, O God; have mercy, O God of gods, O Abode of the universe.<br><br>[sound:gita_11_45.mp3]
gita_verse:11.46	<center><big>किरीटिनं गदिनं चक्रहस्त<br><br>मिच्छामि त्वां द्रष्टुमहं तथैव।<br><br>तेनैव रूपेण चतुर्भुजेन<br><br>सहस्रबाहो भव विश्वमूर्ते।।11.46।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>kirīṭinaṁ gadinaṁ chakra-hastam<br>ichchhāmi tvāṁ draṣhṭum ahaṁ tathaiva<br>tenaiva rūpeṇa chatur-bhujena<br>sahasra-bāho bhava viśhva-mūrte<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>I want to see You just as before, wearing a crown, wielding a mace, and holding a disc in hand. gita_verse:11.47	<center><big>श्री भगवानुवाच<br><br>मया प्रसन्नेन तवार्जुनेदं<br><br>रूपं परं दर्शितमात्मयोगात्।<br><br>तेजोमयं विश्वमनन्तमाद्यं<br><br>यन्मे त्वदन्येन न दृष्टपूर्वम्।।11.47।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>śhrī-bhagavān uvācha<br>mayā prasannena tavārjunedaṁ<br>rūpaṁ paraṁ darśhitam ātma-yogāt<br>tejo-mayaṁ viśhvam anantam ādyaṁ<br>yan me tvad anyena na dṛiṣhṭa-pūrvam<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>The Blessed Lord said, Out of grace, O Arjuna, this supreme, radiant, cosmic, infinite, primeval form—which no one other than you has seen before—has been shown to you by Me through the power of My own Yoga.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>The Blessed Lord said, "O Arjuna, this Cosmic Form has graciously been shown to you by Me through My own Yogic power. gita_verse:11.48	<center><big>न वेदयज्ञाध्ययनैर्न दानै<br><br>र्न च क्रियाभिर्न तपोभिरुग्रैः।<br><br>एवंरूपः शक्य अहं नृलोके<br><br>द्रष्टुं त्वदन्येन कुरुप्रवीर।।11.48।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>na veda-yajñādhyayanair na dānair<br>na cha kriyābhir na tapobhir ugraiḥ<br>evaṁ-rūpaḥ śhakya ahaṁ nṛi-loke<br>draṣhṭuṁ tvad anyena kuru-pravīra<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Not by the study of the Vedas and sacrifices, not by gifts, not even by rituals, nor by severe austerities, can I, in this form, be perceived in the human world by anyone other than you, O most valiant among the Kurus, who has not received My grace.<br><br><b>Devotional — Sivananda:</b><br>Neither by the study of the Vedas, nor by gifts, nor by sacrifices, nor by severe austerities, can I be seen in this form in the world of men by any other than yourself, O great hero of the Kurus (Arjuna).<br><br>[sound:gita_11_48.mp3]
gita_verse:11.49	<center><big>मा ते व्यथा मा च विमूढभावो<br><br>दृष्ट्वा रूपं घोरमीदृङ्ममेदम्।<br><br>व्यपेतभीः प्रीतमनाः पुनस्त्वं<br><br>तदेव मे रूपमिदं प्रपश्य।।11.49।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>mā te vyathā mā cha vimūḍha-bhāvo<br>dṛiṣhṭvā rūpaṁ ghoram īdṛiṅ mamedam<br>vyapeta-bhīḥ prīta-manāḥ punas tvaṁ<br>tad eva me rūpam idaṁ prapaśhya<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>May you have no fear, and may there be no bewilderment upon seeing this form of Mine so terrible. gita_verse:11.50	<center><big>सञ्जय उवाच<br><br>इत्यर्जुनं वासुदेवस्तथोक्त्वा<br><br>स्वकं रूपं दर्शयामास भूयः।<br><br>आश्वासयामास च भीतमेनं<br><br>भूत्वा पुनः सौम्यवपुर्महात्मा।।11.50।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>sañjaya uvācha<br>ity arjunaṁ vāsudevas tathoktvā<br>svakaṁ rūpaṁ darśhayām āsa bhūyaḥ<br>āśhvāsayām āsa cha bhītam enaṁ<br>bhūtvā punaḥ saumya-vapur mahātmā<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>Sanjaya said, Thus, having spoken to Arjuna in that manner, Vasudeva showed His own form again. gita_verse:11.52-53	<center><big>श्री भगवानुवाच<br><br>सुदुर्दर्शमिदं रूपं दृष्टवानसि यन्मम।<br><br>देवा अप्यस्य रूपस्य नित्यं दर्शनकाङ्क्षिणः।।11.52।।<br> <br><br>नाहं वेदैर्न तपसा न दानेन न चेज्यया।<br><br>शक्य एवंविधो द्रष्टुं दृष्टवानसि मां यथा।।11.53।।<br> </big></center>	<b>IAST:</b><br>śhrī-bhagavān uvācha<br>su-durdarśham idaṁ rūpaṁ dṛiṣhṭavān asi yan mama<br>devā apy asya rūpasya nityaṁ darśhana-kāṅkṣhiṇaḥ<br><br>nāhaṁ vedair na tapasā na dānena na chejyayā<br>śhakya evaṁ-vidho draṣhṭuṁ dṛiṣhṭavān asi māṁ yathā<br><br><br><b>Literal — Gambirananda:</b><br>The Blessed Lord said, "This form of Mine, which you have seen, is very difficult to behold; even the gods are ever desirous of a vision of this form."
